### [91] [PTLD: Sim-to-real Privileged Tactile Latent Distillation for Dexterous Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04531)
*Rosy Chen,Mustafa Mukadam,Michael Kaess,Tingfan Wu,Francois R Hogan,Jitendra Malik,Akash Sharma*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了PTLD（特权触觉潜在蒸馏）方法，通过利用真实世界中的特权传感器数据来训练触觉策略，避免了复杂的触觉传感器仿真，在灵巧手操作任务上相比仅用本体感知的方法取得了显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 触觉灵巧操作对自动化复杂家庭任务至关重要，但现有方法存在明显局限：模仿学习需要高质量演示数据，而多指手的遥操作或动觉教学成本高昂；强化学习虽可在仿真中学习技能，但触觉观测的快速真实仿真极具挑战性。

Method: 提出PTLD方法，核心思想是不模拟触觉传感器，而是利用真实世界中的特权传感器收集真实触觉策略数据，然后使用这些数据蒸馏出一个基于触觉输入的鲁棒状态估计器，从而将仿真训练的本体感知策略迁移到真实世界并融合触觉感知。

Result: 在手内旋转基准任务上，PTLD相比仅使用本体感知的策略提升了182%；在更具挑战性的触觉手内重定向任务中，PTLD相比仅用本体感知的方法在达成目标数量上提升了57%。

Conclusion: PTLD成功弥合了仿真与真实世界之间的差距，证明了无需触觉仿真即可有效学习触觉操作技能，显著提升了灵巧手操作任务的性能，为触觉灵巧操作提供了一种实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Tactile dexterous manipulation is essential to automating complex household tasks, yet learning effective control policies remains a challenge. While recent work has relied on imitation learning, obtaining high quality demonstrations for multi-fingered hands via robot teleoperation or kinesthetic teaching is prohibitive. Alternatively, with reinforcement we can learn skills in simulation, but fast and realistic simulation of tactile observations is challenging. To bridge this gap, we introduce PTLD: sim-to-real Privileged Tactile Latent Distillation, a novel approach to learning tactile manipulation skills without requiring tactile simulation. Instead of simulating tactile sensors or relying purely on proprioceptive policies to transfer zero-shot sim-to-real, our key idea is to leverage privileged sensors in the real world to collect real-world tactile policy data. This data is then used to distill a robust state estimator that operates on tactile input. We demonstrate from our experiments that PTLD can be used to improve proprioceptive manipulation policies trained in simulation significantly by incorporating tactile sensing. On the benchmark in-hand rotation task, PTLD achieves a 182% improvement over a proprioception only policy. We also show that PTLD enables learning the challenging task of tactile in-hand reorientation where we see a 57% improvement in the number of goals reached over using proprioception alone. Website: https://akashsharma02.github.io/ptld-website/.

</details>


### [92] [Many-RRT*: Robust Joint-Space Trajectory Planning for Serial Manipulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04547)
*Theodore M. Belmont,Benjamin A. Christie,Anton Netchaev*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出Many-RRT*算法，通过并行规划多个逆运动学目标来解决高自由度机械臂在关节空间规划中的多解问题，显著提升轨迹质量和成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高自由度串联机械臂在关节空间运动规划中面临前向运动学不可逆的挑战：单一任务空间末端位姿可能对应多个构型空间状态，形成多臂老虎机问题。在复杂环境中，选择错误的关节空间目标会导致轨迹次优甚至规划失败。

Method: 提出Many-RRT*算法，扩展自RRT*-Connect。该方法生成多个逆运动学解，从这些目标构型同时生长独立的目标树，并与单一起始树并行规划，确保计算资源不会浪费在次优IK解上。该算法保持鲁棒收敛性和渐近最优性。

Result: 在多种机器人形态和障碍环境下的实验评估表明：Many-RRT*在相同运行时间内轨迹成本降低44.5%，成功率达100%（对比次优方法的1.6%），且不牺牲运行时间性能。

Conclusion: Many-RRT*通过并行规划多个IK目标有效解决了机械臂关节空间规划的多解问题，在轨迹质量和成功率方面显著优于现有RRT变体，同时保持计算效率，为高自由度机械臂运动规划提供了更可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: The rapid advancement of high degree-of-freedom (DoF) serial manipulators necessitates the use of swift, sampling-based motion planners for high-dimensional spaces. While sampling-based planners like the Rapidly-Exploring Random Tree (RRT) are widely used, planning in the manipulator's joint space presents significant challenges due to non-invertible forward kinematics. A single task-space end-effector pose can correspond to multiple configuration-space states, creating a multi-arm bandit problem for the planner. In complex environments, simply choosing the wrong joint space goal can result in suboptimal trajectories or even failure to find a viable plan. To address this planning problem, we propose Many-RRT*: an extension of RRT*-Connect that plans to multiple goals in parallel. By generating multiple IK solutions and growing independent trees from these goal configurations simultaneously alongside a single start tree, Many-RRT* ensures that computational effort is not wasted on suboptimal IK solutions. This approach maintains robust convergence and asymptotic optimality. Experimental evaluations across robot morphologies and diverse obstacle environments demonstrate that Many-RRT* provides higher quality trajectories (44.5% lower cost in the same runtime) with a significantly higher success rate (100% vs. the next best of 1.6%) than previous RRT iterations without compromising on runtime performance.

</details>


### [93] [From Local Corrections to Generalized Skills: Improving Neuro-Symbolic Policies with MEMO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04560)
*Benjamin A. Christie,Yinlong Dai,Mohammad Bararjanianbahnamiri,Simon Stepputtis,Dylan P. Losey*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出MEMO框架，通过收集、聚类和重述多用户自然语言反馈来构建检索增强技能库，动态扩展机器人技能，解决了神经符号框架中技能限制高层策略的关键瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经符号操作策略虽能分解复杂任务，但受限于可用技能：机器人需将语义子任务落地为具体运动，若无法生成正确技能则策略失败。现有技能（轨迹片段、运动基元、编码函数等）构成约束，限制了高层语言推理的落地能力。

Method: 提出Memory Enhanced Manipulation (MEMO)：利用用户反馈动态扩展技能。当机器人失败时，收集人类直观解释（如"不，再高一点"），通过跨多用户和任务收集、聚类、重述自然语言纠正，合成更通用的文本指导和编码技能模板。构建检索增强的技能库，运行时检索相关文本和代码，使策略能基于多任务人类反馈生成新技能。

Result: 实验表明，MEMO将局部反馈聚合为通用技能模板，在新颖任务上实现了现有基线方法无法达到的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 通过系统化利用人类反馈构建和维护技能库，MEMO突破了神经符号框架中技能约束的瓶颈，实现了向新颖任务的泛化，证明了反馈驱动的技能学习在机器人操作中的有效性。

Abstract: Recent works use a neuro-symbolic framework for general manipulation policies. The advantage of this framework is that -- by applying off-the-shelf vision and language models -- the robot can break complex tasks down into semantic subtasks. However, the fundamental bottleneck is that the robot needs skills to ground these subtasks into embodied motions. Skills can take many forms (e.g., trajectory snippets, motion primitives, coded functions), but regardless of their form skills act as a constraint. The high-level policy can only ground its language reasoning through the available skills; if the robot cannot generate the right skill for the current task, its policy will fail. We propose to address this limitation -- and dynamically expand the robot's skills -- by leveraging user feedback. When a robot fails, humans can intuitively explain what went wrong (e.g., ``no, go higher''). While a simple approach is to recall this exact text the next time the robot faces a similar situation, we hypothesize that by collecting, clustering, and re-phrasing natural language corrections across multiple users and tasks, we can synthesize more general text guidance and coded skill templates. Applying this hypothesis we develop Memory Enhanced Manipulation (MEMO). MEMO builds and maintains a retrieval-augmented skillbook gathered from human feedback and task successes. At run time, MEMO retrieves relevant text and code from this skillbook, enabling the robot's policy to generate new skills while reasoning over multi-task human feedback. Our experiments demonstrate that using MEMO to aggregate local feedback into general skill templates enables generalization to novel tasks where existing baselines fall short. See supplemental material here: https://collab.me.vt.edu/memo

</details>

Method: 各无人机利用机载单目相机检测载荷上的基准标记并估计相对位姿，通过分布式去中心化扩展信息滤波（DDEIF）融合多机测量数据，实现可扩展且对单传感器故障具有韧性的载荷状态估计，并用于闭环轨迹跟踪控制。

Abstract: Transporting heavy or oversized slung loads using rotorcraft has traditionally relied on single-aircraft systems, which limits both payload capacity and control authority. Most prior multilift research assumes GPS availability, uses centralized estimation architectures, or relies on controlled laboratory motion-capture setups. ### [96] [Risk-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Mobile Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04579)
*Michael Groom,James Wilson,Nick Hawes,Lars Kunze*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文首次提出了一种基于模仿学习的风险感知视觉运动策略，用于移动操作任务。该方法通过分布式强化学习训练特权教师策略，应用失真风险度量实现运行时可调的风险敏感性，并通过模仿学习将其迁移到基于自我中心深度观测的学生策略中，在未知环境中实现了更好的最坏情况性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有移动操作机器人的全身控制器缺乏在不确定性下进行风险敏感决策的显式机制。为了使机器人能够从实验室环境成功过渡到日常环境，必须具备推理动作相关风险并做出明智的风险感知决策的能力，特别是在涉及交互和导航的动态、非结构化空间中执行移动操作任务时。

Method: 1. 使用分布式强化学习(DRL)训练特权教师策略，采用风险中性的分布式评论器；2. 对评论器预测的回报分布应用失真风险度量，计算风险调整的优势估计用于策略更新；3. 通过模仿学习将教师策略蒸馏为基于自我中心深度观测的风险感知学生策略。该方法实现了运行时可调的风险敏感性。

Result: 广泛的评估表明，训练的视觉运动策略在未知环境中执行反应性全身运动时表现出风险感知行为，具体实现了更好的最坏情况性能，同时利用实时深度观测进行感知。该方法成功展示了风险感知行为可以通过模仿学习迁移到基于自我中心深度观测的视觉运动策略中。

Conclusion: 本研究首次实现了基于自我中心深度观测的移动操作风险感知视觉运动策略，并证明了风险感知行为可以通过模仿学习有效迁移。该方法为机器人在真实世界动态环境中的安全部署提供了新的技术途径，使机器人能够在不确定性下做出更稳健的决策。

Abstract: For robots to successfully transition from lab settings to everyday environments, they must begin to reason about the risks associated with their actions and make informed, risk-aware decisions. This is particularly true for robots performing mobile manipulation tasks, which involve both interacting with and navigating within dynamic, unstructured spaces. However, existing whole-body controllers for mobile manipulators typically lack explicit mechanisms for risk-sensitive decision-making under uncertainty. To our knowledge, we are the first to (i) learn risk-aware visuomotor policies for mobile manipulation conditioned on egocentric depth observations with runtime-adjustable risk sensitivity, and (ii) show risk-aware behaviours can be transferred through Imitation Learning (IL) to a visuomotor policy conditioned on egocentric depth observations. Our method achieves this by first training a privileged teacher policy using Distributional Reinforcement Learning (DRL), with a risk-neutral distributional critic. Distortion risk-metrics are then applied to the critic's predicted return distribution to calculate risk-adjusted advantage estimates used in policy updates to achieve a range of risk-aware behaviours. We then distil teacher policies with IL to obtain risk-aware student policies conditioned on egocentric depth observations. We perform extensive evaluations demonstrating that our trained visuomotor policies exhibit risk-aware behaviour (specifically achieving better worst-case performance) while performing reactive whole-body motions in unmapped environments, leveraging live depth observations for perception.

### [97] [ELLIPSE: Evidential Learning for Robust Waypoints and Uncertainties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04585)
*Zihao Dong,Chanyoung Chung,Dong-Ki Kim,Mukhtar Maulimov,Xiangyun Meng,Harmish Khambhaita,Ali-akbar Agha-mohammadi,Amirreza Shaban*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了ELLIPSE方法，基于多元深度证据回归实现鲁棒的航点预测与不确定性估计，通过域增强和后验重校准技术解决了模仿学习在开放世界中的分布偏移和过度自信问题，在楼梯航点预测任务上显著提升了成功率与不确定性覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开放世界和安全关键场景中，移动机器人的航点预测需要具备鲁棒性。现有的模仿学习方法虽然表现良好，但在遇到分布偏移时容易变得过度自信，导致在陌生状态下产生危险行为。这一问题的核心挑战在于：协变量偏移（如视点和姿态扰动）会引发过度自信，而环境/域偏移（如未见过的楼梯）会降低不确定性估计的可靠性。

Method: ELLIPSE方法包含三个核心组件：(1) 基于多元深度证据回归的模型，可在单次前向传播中输出航点预测和多元Student-t预测分布；(2) 轻量级域增强过程，通过合成合理的视点/姿态变化来减少专家轨迹附近的协变量偏移引发的过度自信，无需收集额外演示数据；(3) 基于概率积分变换(PIT)值的事后保序重校准，确保在环境/域偏移下预测集合保持合理性。方法在楼梯航点预测场景中进行验证。

Result: 在真实世界的广泛评估中，ELLIPSE相比基线方法在任务成功率和不确定性覆盖率方面均有显著提升。实验结果表明该方法能够有效处理视点、姿态扰动以及未见环境场景下的鲁棒航点预测与不确定性估计问题。

Conclusion: ELLIPSE成功解决了模仿学习中分布偏移导致的过度自信问题，通过多元证据回归、域增强和后验重校准的协同作用，实现了安全关键场景下更可靠、更鲁棒的航点预测，为移动机器人在开放世界中的安全部署提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Robust waypoint prediction is crucial for mobile robots operating in open-world, safety-critical settings. While Imitation Learning (IL) methods have demonstrated great success in practice, they are susceptible to distribution shifts: the policy can become dangerously overconfident in unfamiliar states. In this paper, we present \textit{ELLIPSE}, a method building on multivariate deep evidential regression to output waypoints and multivariate Student-t predictive distributions in a single forward pass. To reduce covariate-shift-induced overconfidence under viewpoint and pose perturbations near expert trajectories, we introduce a lightweight domain augmentation procedure that synthesizes plausible viewpoint/pose variations without collecting additional demonstrations. To improve uncertainty reliability under environment/domain shift (e.g., unseen staircases), we apply a post-hoc isotonic recalibration on probability integral transform (PIT) values so that prediction sets remain plausible during deployment. We ground the discussion and experiments in staircase waypoint prediction, where obtaining robust waypoint and uncertainty is pivotal. Extensive real world evaluations show that \textit{ELLIPSE} improves both task success rate and uncertainty coverage compared to baselines.

This limits their systematic understanding, comparison, and progress measurement. To address these challenges, we introduce RoboMME: a large-scale standardized benchmark for evaluating and advancing VLA models in long-horizon, history-dependent scenarios. Our benchmark comprises 16 manipulation tasks constructed under a carefully designed taxonomy that evaluates temporal, spatial, object, and procedural memory. We further develop a suite of 14 memory-augmented VLA variants built on the π0.5 backbone to systematically explore different memory representations across multiple integration strategies. Videos and code can be found at our website https://robomme.github.io.

### [101] [Python Bindings for a Large C++ Robotics Library: The Case of OMPL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04668)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种人机协作工作流程：1) 镜像C++代码库结构；2) 搭建空的包装器文件脚手架；3) 使用LLM填充绑定定义；4) 专家审查和优化生成的代码以确保正确性、兼容性和性能。采用上下文示例和精心设计的提示来提高可靠性。

Result: 在一个大型C++运动规划库的案例研究中，记录了常见失败模式（包括共享指针管理不当、重载问题和trampolines问题），并展示了上下文示例和提示设计如何提高可靠性。实验表明，生成的绑定在运行时性能上与传统解决方案相当。

Abstract: Python bindings are a critical bridge between high-performance C++ libraries and the flexibility of Python, enabling rapid prototyping, reproducible experiments, and integration with simulation and learning frameworks in robotics research. Yet, generating bindings for large codebases is a tedious process that creates a heavy burden for a small group of maintainers. In this work, we investigate the use of Large Language Models (LLMs) to assist in generating nanobind wrappers, with human experts kept in the loop. Our workflow mirrors the structure of the C++ codebase, scaffolds empty wrapper files, and employs LLMs to fill in binding definitions. Experts then review and refine the generated code to ensure correctness, compatibility, and performance. Through a case study on a large C++ motion planning library, we document common failure modes, including mismanaging shared pointers, overloads, and trampolines, and show how in-context examples and careful prompt design improve reliability. Experiments demonstrate that the resulting bindings achieve runtime performance comparable to legacy solutions. Beyond this case study, our results provide general lessons for applying LLMs to binding generation in large-scale C++ projects.

*Long Kiu Chung,David Isele,Faizan M. Tariq,Sangjae Bae,Shreyas Kousik,Jovin D'sa*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文针对自主代客泊车（AVP）场景，提出了一种通过显式预测其他车辆泊车意图来选择停车位的管道方法。该方法利用运动历史和概率信念图进行意图预测，在仿真实验中优于从短期运动预测推断意图或端到端隐式建模的现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自主代客泊车场景中，驾驶规则相对宽松，车辆具有多样且模糊的长期目标。现有方法仅从短期运动预测推断意图或通过端到端模型隐式嵌入意图，难以可靠地推理这些长期目标，因此需要显式的意图预测来提升决策的安全性和社会接受度。

Method: 提出一个AVP管道，通过学习模型和概率信念图，利用其他智能体的运动历史显式预测其泊车位置，从而选择停车位。构建了包含反应式智能体、遮挡感知观测和不完美轨迹预测等现实假设的仿真环境进行测试。

Result: 仿真实验表明，该方法在预测准确性、社会接受度和任务完成率方面均优于从未来预测运动推断意图或将意图隐式嵌入端到端模型的现有工作。

Conclusion: 在泊车等驾驶规则宽松的场景中，显式意图预测对于推理多样且模糊的长期目标至关重要。短期运动预测无法可靠推断此类目标，但可以通过运动历史有效学习，从而提升自主泊车的性能。

Abstract: In many applications of social navigation, existing works have shown that predicting and reasoning about human intentions can help robotic agents make safer and more socially acceptable decisions. In this work, we study this problem for autonomous valet parking (AVP), where an autonomous vehicle ego agent must drop off its passengers, explore the parking lot, find a parking spot, negotiate for the spot with other vehicles, and park in the spot without human supervision. Specifically, we propose an AVP pipeline that selects parking spots by explicitly predicting where other agents are going to park from their motion history using learned models and probabilistic belief maps. To test this pipeline, we build a simulation environment with reactive agents and realistic modeling assumptions on the ego agent, such as occlusion-aware observations, and imperfect trajectory prediction. Simulation experiments show that our proposed method outperforms existing works that infer intentions from future predicted motion or embed them implicitly in end-to-end models, yielding better results in prediction accuracy, social acceptance, and task completion. Our key insight is that, in parking, where driving regulations are more lax, explicit intention prediction is crucial for reasoning about diverse and ambiguous long-term goals, which cannot be reliably inferred from short-term motion prediction alone, but can be effectively learned from motion history.

### [103] [LEGS-POMDP: Language and Gesture-Guided Object Search in Partially Observable Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04705)
*Ivy Xiao He,Stefanie Tellex,Jason Xinyu Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了LEGS-POMDP，一个融合语言、手势和视觉观测的模块化POMDP系统，用于开放世界中的目标搜索任务。该系统显式建模目标对象身份和空间位置的不确定性，在仿真中达到89%的平均成功率，并在四足移动机械臂上完成了真实世界验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于基础模型的方法在多模态grounding方面表现出色，但在长视野任务中缺乏建模不确定性的原则性机制；而POMDP虽提供了不确定性下规划的系统性框架，但受限于支持的模态较少且依赖严格的环境假设。两者在开放世界对象搜索任务中均存在不足。

Method: 提出LEGS-POMDP（LanguagE and Gesture-Guided Object Search in Partially Observable Environments），一个模块化的POMDP系统。该系统整合语言、手势和视觉三种模态观测，显式建模两种部分可观测性来源：目标对象身份的不确定性和空间位置的不确定性。通过多模态融合实现开放世界对象搜索。

Result: 在仿真实验中，多模态融合方法显著优于单模态基线方法，在具有挑战性的环境和对象类别上达到89%的平均成功率。在四足移动机械臂平台上进行的真实世界实验定性地验证了该方法在模糊指令下具有鲁棒的多模态感知能力和不确定性降低效果。

Conclusion: LEGS-POMDP成功弥合了基础模型方法与POMDP框架之间的差距，为开放世界环境中处理模糊指令的对象搜索任务提供了一个有效的解决方案，证明了显式建模双重不确定性（对象身份和空间位置）的重要性。

Abstract: To assist humans in open-world environments, robots must interpret ambiguous instructions to locate desired objects. Foundation model-based approaches excel at multimodal grounding, but they lack a principled mechanism for modeling uncertainty in long-horizon tasks. In contrast, Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs) provide a systematic framework for planning under uncertainty but are often limited in supported modalities and rely on restrictive environment assumptions. We introduce LanguagE and Gesture-Guided Object Search in Partially Observable Environments (LEGS-POMDP), a modular POMDP system that integrates language, gesture, and visual observations for open-world object search. Unlike prior work, LEGS-POMDP explicitly models two sources of partial observability: uncertainty over the target object's identity and its spatial location. In simulation, multimodal fusion significantly outperforms unimodal baselines, achieving an average success rate of 89\% across challenging environments and object categories. Finally, we demonstrate the full system on a quadruped mobile manipulator, where real-world experiments qualitatively validate robust multimodal perception and uncertainty reduction under ambiguous instructions.

Method: 开发了GenTact-Prox人工皮肤平台，采用模块化设计，可程序化生成以适应任意机器人形态，集成触觉和接近感知功能；引入数据驱动框架来映射感知周围空间（Perisensory Space），即传感器为接触预判提供可操作信息的身体中心空间区域。

Abstract: Robots operating in dynamic and shared environments benefit from anticipating contact before it occurs. We present GenTact-Prox, a fully 3D-printed artificial skin that integrates tactile and proximity sensing for contact detection and anticipation. The artificial skin platform is modular in design, procedurally generated to fit any robot morphology, and can cover the whole body of a robot. The skin achieved detection ranges of up to 18 cm during evaluation. To characterize how robots perceive nearby space through this skin, we introduce a data-driven framework for mapping the Perisensory Space -- the body-centric volume of space around the robot where sensors provide actionable information for contact anticipation. We demonstrate this approach on a Franka Research 3 robot equipped with five GenTact-Prox units, enabling online object-aware operation and contact prediction.

Conclusion: 所提出的优化框架能够有效降低模块化机器人关节负载风险，在保证运动性能的前提下确保结构完整性，为模块化机器人在复杂环境中的可靠运行提供了可行方案。

Unlike conventional approaches that prioritize mobility alone, our method derives Pareto optimal solutions to minimize joint load while maintaining necessary locomotion speed and stability. Simulations and physical experiments demonstrate that our approach successfully generates gait motions for diverse environments, such as slopes and steps, ensuring structural integrity without compromising overall mobility.

To make this autonomous exchange practically feasible, the mechanism is complemented by a compact rotating tool exchange station for efficient module storage. ### [107] [Adaptive Policy Switching of Two-Wheeled Differential Robots for Traversing over Diverse Terrains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04761)
*Haruki Izawa,Takeshi Takai,Shingo Kitano,Mikita Miyaguchi,Hiroaki Kawashima*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 月球熔岩管探索需要机器人在无人类干预的情况下自主穿越复杂地形。由于预训练策略无法覆盖所有可能的地形条件，研究动机是使机器人能够根据当前地形特征选择合适的专业化模型，实现自适应策略切换。

Method: 该方法首先使用近端策略优化（PPO）微调预训练策略，然后在仿真熔岩管环境中收集机器人在平坦和粗糙地形上导航时的3D姿态数据。通过分析发现机器人俯仰角数据的标准差在这两种地形类型间存在明显差异。采用高斯混合模型（GMM）对不同窗口大小下的地形进行分类评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，使用70步窗口时，地形分类准确率超过98%。研究发现短期姿态数据足以实现可靠的地形估计，为自适应策略切换提供了基础。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于机器人短期姿态数据（特别是俯仰角标准差）进行地形分类的可行性，为实现月球熔岩管探索中的自适应策略切换提供了有效方法和技术基础。

Abstract: Exploring lunar lava tubes requires robots to traverse without human intervention. Because pre-trained policies cannot fully cover all possible terrain conditions, our goal is to enable adaptive policy switching, where the robot selects an appropriate terrain-specialized model based on its current terrain features. This study investigates whether terrain types can be estimated effectively using posture-related observations collected during navigation. We fine-tuned a pre-trained policy using Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), and then collected the robot's 3D orientation data as it moved across flat and rough terrain in a simulated lava-tube environment. Our analysis revealed that the standard deviation of the robot's pitch data shows a clear difference between these two terrain types. Using Gaussian mixture models (GMM), we evaluated terrain classification across various window sizes. An accuracy of more than 98% was achieved when using a 70-step window. The result suggests that short-term orientation data are sufficient for reliable terrain estimation, providing a foundation for adaptive policy switching.

### [108] [Data-Driven Control of a Magnetically Actuated Fish-Like Robot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04787)
*Akiyuki Koyama,Hiroaki Kawashima*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于磁驱动仿生鱼机器人的数据驱动控制框架。该方法结合了基于神经网络的动力学模型、梯度模型预测控制（G-MPC）以及模仿学习，在无需解析建模的情况下实现了精确的路径跟踪控制，并有效降低了实时计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁驱动仿生鱼机器人为水下探测提供了小型化、高灵活性的解决方案。然而，由于非线性流体动力学、柔性鳍迟滞效应以及驱动机制固有的变时长控制步长等复杂因素，实现精确控制仍然是一个重大挑战。传统的解析建模方法难以有效应对这些复杂性。

Method: 提出了一个包含三个核心组件的数据驱动控制框架：1）利用神经网络在真实实验数据上训练前向动力学模型（FDM），以捕捉不同时间步长下的状态转移；2）将FDM集成到基于梯度的模型预测控制（G-MPC）架构中，优化路径跟踪的控制输入；3）应用模仿学习近似G-MPC策略，从而降低实时部署的计算成本。

Result: 通过使用辨识得到的动力学模型进行仿真验证，结果表明G-MPC框架实现了准确的路径收敛，具有极小的均方根误差（RMSE）；同时，模仿学习控制器（ILC）能够有效复现G-MPC的控制性能。

Conclusion: 本研究验证了数据驱动控制策略在实现微型软体仿生鱼机器人精确导航方面的潜力，为解决复杂非线性系统的控制问题提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Magnetically actuated fish-like robots offer promising solutions for underwater exploration due to their miniaturization and agility; however, precise control remains a significant challenge because of nonlinear fluid dynamics, flexible fin hysteresis, and the variable-duration control steps inherent to the actuation mechanism. This paper proposes a comprehensive data-driven control framework to address these complexities without relying on analytical modeling. Our methodology comprises three core components: 1) developing a forward dynamics model (FDM) using a neural network trained on real-world experimental data to capture state transitions under varying time steps; 2) integrating this FDM into a gradient-based model predictive control (G-MPC) architecture to optimize control inputs for path following; and 3) applying imitation learning to approximate the G-MPC policy, thereby reducing the computational cost for real-time implementation. We validate the approach through simulations utilizing the identified dynamics model. The results demonstrate that the G-MPC framework achieves accurate path convergence with minimal root mean square error (RMSE), and the imitation learning controller (ILC) effectively replicates this performance. This study highlights the potential of data-driven control strategies for the precise navigation of miniature, fish-like soft robots.

</details>


### [109] [On the Strengths and Weaknesses of Data for Open-set Embodied Assistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04819)
*Pradyumna Tambwekar,Andrew Silva,Deepak Gopinath,Jonathan DeCastro,Xiongyi Cui,Guy Rosman*

Main category: cs.RO

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出开放集纠正辅助任务，要求模型检查用户行为并提供纠正性动作或语言反馈；在Overcooked合成环境中生成辅助数据集；基于LLaMA架构微调多模态基础模型；从两个维度评估泛化能力：未见过的用户行为类别和训练时未遇到的配置场景。

Result: 实验表明，性能优异的模型得益于覆盖辅助任务不同方面的数据集，包括多模态接地能力、缺陷推理能力和多样化场景暴露；模型能够有效泛化到新任务和新用户行为，为开放集辅助智能提供了关键见解。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了构建有效辅助数据集的关键要素，证明了多样化交互数据对提升具身基础模型泛化能力的重要性，为未来开发开放集辅助智能系统提供了理论和实践指导。

Abstract: Embodied foundation models are increasingly performant in real-world domains such as robotics or autonomous driving. These models are often deployed in interactive or assistive settings, where it is important that these assistive models generalize to new users and new tasks. Diverse interactive data generation offers a promising avenue for providing data-efficient generalization capabilities for interactive embodied foundation models. In this paper, we investigate the generalization capabilities of a multimodal foundation model fine-tuned on diverse interactive assistance data in a synthetic domain. We explore generalization along two axes: a) assistance with unseen categories of user behavior and b) providing guidance in new configurations not encountered during training. We study a broad capability called \textbf{Open-Set Corrective Assistance}, in which the model needs to inspect lengthy user behavior and provide assistance through either corrective actions or language-based feedback. This task remains unsolved in prior work, which typically assumes closed corrective categories or relies on external planners, making it a challenging testbed for evaluating the limits of assistive data. To support this task, we generate synthetic assistive datasets in Overcooked and fine-tune a LLaMA-based model to evaluate generalization to novel tasks and user behaviors. Our approach provides key insights into the nature of assistive datasets required to enable open-set assistive intelligence. In particular, we show that performant models benefit from datasets that cover different aspects of assistance, including multimodal grounding, defect inference, and exposure to diverse scenarios.

### [110] [Task-Relevant and Irrelevant Region-Aware Augmentation for Generalizable Vision-Based Imitation Learning in Agricultural Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04845)
*Shun Hattori,Hikaru Sasaki,Takumi Hachimine,Yusuke Mizutani,Takamitsu Matsubara*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为DRAIL的双区域增强框架，通过将视觉观察分离为任务相关和任务无关区域并分别进行不同策略的数据增强，有效提升了农业机器人操作任务中视觉模仿学习的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉模仿学习在农业机器人操作任务中泛化能力有限，主要面临两个挑战：演示数据稀缺，以及由作物外观多样性和背景变化引起的显著视觉域差距。

Method: 提出双区域增强模仿学习（DRAIL）框架，将视觉观察显式分离为任务相关区域和任务无关区域。对任务相关区域采用领域知识驱动的增强方式以保留关键视觉特征，对任务无关区域进行激进随机化以抑制虚假背景关联。

Result: 在基于扩散策略的视觉运动控制器上进行了人工蔬菜采摘和真实生菜残叶拣选准备任务的机器人实验。结果显示，在未见过的视觉条件下，相比基线方法成功率得到持续提升。注意力分析和表示泛化指标表明，学习到的策略更依赖于任务关键视觉特征。

Conclusion: DRAIL通过联合处理两种视觉变化源，有效促进了策略学习依赖于任务本质特征而非偶然视觉线索，显著增强了农业操作任务中视觉模仿学习的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Vision-based imitation learning has shown promise for robotic manipulation; however, its generalization remains limited in practical agricultural tasks. This limitation stems from scarce demonstration data and substantial visual domain gaps caused by i) crop-specific appearance diversity and ii) background variations. To address this limitation, we propose Dual-Region Augmentation for Imitation Learning (DRAIL), a region-aware augmentation framework designed for generalizable vision-based imitation learning in agricultural manipulation. DRAIL explicitly separates visual observations into task-relevant and task-irrelevant regions. The task-relevant region is augmented in a domain-knowledge-driven manner to preserve essential visual characteristics, while the task-irrelevant region is aggressively randomized to suppress spurious background correlations. By jointly handling both sources of visual variation, DRAIL promotes learning policies that rely on task-essential features rather than incidental visual cues. We evaluate DRAIL on diffusion policy-based visuomotor controllers through robot experiments on artificial vegetable harvesting and real lettuce defective leaf picking preparation tasks. The results show consistent improvements in success rates under unseen visual conditions compared to baseline methods. Further attention analysis and representation generalization metrics indicate that the learned policies rely more on task-essential visual features, resulting in enhanced robustness and generalization.

</details>

*Jin Yang,Ping Wei,Yixin Chen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出HyperMVP框架，扩展掩码自编码器范式，设计GeoLink编码器学习多视角双曲表示；引入大规模3D点云数据集3D-MOV支持预训练；预训练后的编码器在操作任务上与视觉运动策略进行微调。

Result: 在COLOSSEUM、RLBench和真实场景上的实验表明，HyperMVP在多种任务和干扰设置下均持续优于强基线方法，验证了非欧几里得空间中3D感知预训练的有效性。

Conclusion: 双曲空间中的3D感知预训练能够学习到更鲁棒、更具泛化能力的机器人操作策略，为机器人视觉表示学习提供了新的方向。

Abstract: 3D-aware visual pretraining has proven effective in improving the performance of downstream robotic manipulation tasks. However, existing methods are constrained to Euclidean embedding spaces, whose flat geometry limits their ability to model structural relations among embeddings. As a result, they struggle to learn structured embeddings that are essential for robust spatial perception in robotic applications. To this end, we propose HyperMVP, a self-supervised framework for \underline{Hyper}bolic \underline{M}ulti\underline{V}iew \underline{P}retraining. Hyperbolic space offers geometric properties well suited for capturing structural relations. Methodologically, we extend the masked autoencoder paradigm and design a GeoLink encoder to learn multiview hyperbolic representations. The pretrained encoder is then finetuned with visuomotor policies on manipulation tasks. In addition, we introduce 3D-MOV, a large-scale dataset comprising multiple types of 3D point clouds to support pretraining. We evaluate HyperMVP on COLOSSEUM, RLBench, and real-world scenarios, where it consistently outperforms strong baselines across diverse tasks and perturbation settings. Our results highlight the potential of 3D-aware pretraining in a non-Euclidean space for learning robust and generalizable robotic manipulation policies.

### [112] [VPWEM: Non-Markovian Visuomotor Policy with Working and Episodic Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04910)
*Yuheng Lei,Zhixuan Liang,Hongyuan Zhang,Ping Luo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出VPWEM，一种结合工作记忆和情节记忆的非马尔可夫视觉-运动策略，通过Transformer压缩器将历史观测压缩为固定数量的记忆标记，在保持常数级计算和内存开销的同时，显著提升了长时记忆密集型任务的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模仿学习方法多基于单步观测或短上下文，难以处理需要长期记忆的非马尔可夫任务；简单扩大上下文窗口会带来巨大的计算和内存开销，并导致过拟合虚假相关性和分布偏移下的灾难性失败。

Method: 提出VPWEM框架，包含两个核心组件：（1）滑动窗口工作记忆保留近期观测标记作为短期记忆；（2）基于Transformer的情节记忆压缩器，递归地将窗口外的观测压缩为固定数量的情节记忆标记。压缩器采用自注意力处理历史摘要缓存和交叉注意力处理历史观测缓存，并与策略联合训练。在扩散策略上进行实例化，利用短期和全局信息生成动作。

Result: 在MIKASA记忆密集型操作任务上，VPWEM比扩散策略和视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型等最先进基线性能提升超过20%；在移动操作基准MoMaRT上平均提升5%，同时每步仅需近似常数的内存和计算开销。

Conclusion: VPWEM成功地将人类的记忆压缩机制引入机器人学习，通过工作记忆与情节记忆的结合有效解决了长时依赖问题，为非马尔可夫任务提供了高效、可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Imitation learning from human demonstrations has achieved significant success in robotic control, yet most visuomotor policies still condition on single-step observations or short-context histories, making them struggle with non-Markovian tasks that require long-term memory. Simply enlarging the context window incurs substantial computational and memory costs and encourages overfitting to spurious correlations, leading to catastrophic failures under distribution shift and violating real-time constraints in robotic systems. By contrast, humans can compress important past experiences into long-term memories and exploit them to solve tasks throughout their lifetime. In this paper, we propose VPWEM, a non-Markovian visuomotor policy equipped with working and episodic memories. VPWEM retains a sliding window of recent observation tokens as short-term working memory, and introduces a Transformer-based contextual memory compressor that recursively converts out-of-window observations into a fixed number of episodic memory tokens. The compressor uses self-attention over a cache of past summary tokens and cross-attention over a cache of historical observations, and is trained jointly with the policy. We instantiate VPWEM on diffusion policies to exploit both short-term and episode-wide information for action generation with nearly constant memory and computation per step. Experiments demonstrate that VPWEM outperforms state-of-the-art baselines including diffusion policies and vision-language-action (VLA) models by more than 20% on the memory-intensive manipulation tasks in MIKASA and achieves an average 5% improvement on the mobile manipulation benchmark MoMaRT. Code is available at https://github.com/HarryLui98/code_vpwem.

</details>


### [113] [Beyond the Patch: Exploring Vulnerabilities of Visuomotor Policies via Viewpoint-Consistent 3D Adversarial Object](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04913)
*Chanmi Lee,Minsung Yoon,Woojae Kim,Sebin Lee,Sung-eui Yoon*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于神经网络的 visuomotor 策略容易受到感知攻击，但传统的2D对抗补丁在固定相机设置下有效，而在动态视角（如手腕安装相机）下因透视失真而效果下降。为了主动研究超越2D补丁的潜在漏洞，需要开发能在不同视角下保持有效性的对抗性攻击方法。

Method: 提出了一种通过可微渲染为3D物体生成视点一致性对抗纹理的优化方法。采用期望变换（EOT）结合从粗到细（C2F）的课程学习策略，利用距离依赖的频率特性来生成在不同相机-物体距离下有效的纹理。进一步集成显著性引导的扰动来重定向策略注意力，并设计了目标损失函数以持续驱动机器人朝向对抗物体。

Result: 全面的实验表明，所提出的方法在各种环境条件下均有效，同时验证了其黑盒迁移能力和现实世界的适用性。该方法成功地在动态视角下生成了有效的对抗性纹理。

Conclusion: 本研究为研究机器人 visuomotor 策略的潜在脆弱性提供了新的视角，证明了3D对抗纹理相比传统2D补丁具有更强的鲁棒性和泛化能力，为机器人系统的安全性评估提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Neural network-based visuomotor policies enable robots to perform manipulation tasks but remain susceptible to perceptual attacks. For example, conventional 2D adversarial patches are effective under fixed-camera setups, where appearance is relatively consistent; however, their efficacy often diminishes under dynamic viewpoints from moving cameras, such as wrist-mounted setups, due to perspective distortions. To proactively investigate potential vulnerabilities beyond 2D patches, this work proposes a viewpoint-consistent adversarial texture optimization method for 3D objects through differentiable rendering. As optimization strategies, we employ Expectation over Transformation (EOT) with a Coarse-to-Fine (C2F) curriculum, exploiting distance-dependent frequency characteristics to induce textures effective across varying camera-object distances. We further integrate saliency-guided perturbations to redirect policy attention and design a targeted loss that persistently drives robots toward adversarial objects. Our comprehensive experiments show that the proposed method is effective under various environmental conditions, while confirming its black-box transferability and real-world applicability.

### [114] [U-OBCA: Uncertainty-Aware Optimization-Based Collision Avoidance via Wasserstein Distributionally Robust Chance Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04914)
*Zehao Wang,Yuxuan Tang,Han Zhang,Jingchuan Wang,Weidong Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了U-OBCA方法，一种扩展的基于优化的避碰框架，通过基于OBCA的机会约束显式处理多边形机器人与障碍物之间的碰撞风险，避免了传统几何简化带来的过度保守性，在狭窄拥挤环境中显著提升了导航效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有不确定性感知规划器通常使用圆形或椭圆等简单几何图元近似多边形机器人和障碍物，虽然计算方便，但大幅缩小了可行空间，导致轨迹过于保守甚至在狭窄环境中规划失败。此外，许多方法依赖特定的噪声分布假设，限制了其在实际应用中的性能保证。

Method: 将基于优化的避碰（OBCA）框架扩展为不确定性感知形式（U-OBCA），通过基于OBCA的机会约束显式建模多边形机器人与障碍物之间的碰撞风险。在温和的分布假设下，将这些概率约束紧化为确定性非线性约束，可由标准数值优化求解器高效求解。

Result: 通过理论分析、数值仿真和真实世界实验验证，U-OBCA显著缓解了轨迹规划中的保守性，相比现有基线方法实现了更高的导航效率，尤其在狭窄和拥挤环境中表现优异。

Conclusion: U-OBCA成功解决了现有不确定性感知规划方法中的几何近似和分布假设限制问题，通过显式处理多边形碰撞风险，避免了不必要的保守性，为机器人在不确定环境下的安全导航提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Uncertainties arising from localization error, trajectory prediction errors of the moving obstacles and environmental disturbances pose significant challenges to robot's safe navigation. Existing uncertainty-aware planners often approximate polygon-shaped robots and obstacles using simple geometric primitives such as circles or ellipses. Though computationally convenient, these approximations substantially shrink the feasible space, leading to overly conservative trajectories and even planning failure in narrow environments. In addition, many such methods rely on specific assumptions about noise distributions, which may not hold in practice and thus limit their performance guarantees. To address these limitations, we extend the Optimization-Based Collision Avoidance (OBCA) framework to an uncertainty-aware formulation, termed \emph{U-OBCA}. The proposed method explicitly accounts for the collision risk between polygon-shaped robots and obstacles by formulating OBCA-based chance constraints, and hence avoiding geometric simplifications and reducing unnecessary conservatism. These probabilistic constraints are further tightened into deterministic nonlinear constraints under mild distributional assumptions, which can be solved efficiently by standard numerical optimization solvers. The proposed approach is validated through theoretical analysis, numerical simulations and real-world experiments. The results demonstrate that U-OBCA significantly mitigates the conservatism in trajectory planning and achieves higher navigation efficiency compared to existing baseline methods, particularly in narrow and cluttered environments.

### [117] [Direct Contact-Tolerant Motion Planning With Vision Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05017)
*He Li,Jian Sun,Chengyang Li,Guoliang Li,Qiyu Ruan,Shuai Wang,Chengzhong Xu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种直接接触容忍（DCT）规划器，通过将视觉-语言模型（VLM）集成到直接点感知与导航中，解决了现有接触容忍运动规划方法在杂乱环境中依赖间接空间表示导致的不准确和缺乏适应性问题，实现了更高效稳健的导航。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在杂乱环境中导航时，机器人经常需要与可移动或可变形物体发生接触以保持效率。现有的接触容忍运动规划（CTMP）方法依赖间接空间表示（如预建地图、障碍物集合），导致不准确且缺乏对环境不确定性的适应性。

Method: 提出直接接触容忍（DCT）规划器，包含两个核心组件：（1）VLM点云分割器（VPP）：利用VLM在图像空间进行接触容忍推理，缓存推理掩码，通过里程计在帧间传播，并投影到当前扫描以生成接触感知点云；（2）VPP引导导航（VGN）：将CTMP表述为直接接触感知点云约束下的感知到控制优化问题，并通过专门的深度神经网络（DNN）求解。

Result: 在Isaac Sim仿真环境和真实类车机器人上实施DCT，实验表明DCT在包含可移动障碍物的杂乱环境中实现了稳健高效的导航，在多项指标上优于代表性基线方法。

Conclusion: DCT规划器通过将VLM集成到直接感知与导航框架中，有效解决了传统CTMP方法的局限性，为机器人在杂乱动态环境中的接触容忍导航提供了新的解决方案，代码已开源。

Abstract: Navigation in cluttered environments often requires robots to tolerate contact with movable or deformable objects to maintain efficiency. Existing contact-tolerant motion planning (CTMP) methods rely on indirect spatial representations (e.g., prebuilt map, obstacle set), resulting in inaccuracies and a lack of adaptiveness to environmental uncertainties. To address this issue, we propose a direct contact-tolerant (DCT) planner, which integrates vision-language models (VLMs) into direct point perception and navigation, including two key components. The first one is VLM point cloud partitioner (VPP), which performs contact-tolerance reasoning in image space using VLM, caches inference masks, propagates them across frames using odometry, and projects them onto the current scan to generate a contact-aware point cloud. The second innovation is VPP guided navigation (VGN), which formulates CTMP as a perception-to-control optimization problem under direct contact-aware point cloud constraints, which is further solved by a specialized deep neural network (DNN). We implement DCT in Isaac Sim and a real car-like robot, demonstrating that DCT achieves robust and efficient navigation in cluttered environments with movable obstacles, outperforming representative baselines across diverse metrics. The code is available at: https://github.com/ChrisLeeUM/DCT.

</details>

Conclusion: VinePT-Map框架适用于农业环境中的长期自主作业，能够有效应对季节变化带来的挑战，为农业机器人的可靠部署提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Reliable long-term deployment of autonomous robots in agricultural environments remains challenging due to perceptual aliasing, seasonal variability, and the dynamic nature of crop canopies. Vineyards, characterized by repetitive row structures and significant visual changes across phenological stages, represent a pivotal field challenge, limiting the robustness of conventional feature-based localization and mapping approaches. This paper introduces VinePT-Map, a semantic mapping framework that leverages vine trunks and support poles as persistent structural landmarks to enable season-agnostic and resilient robot localization. The proposed method formulates the mapping problem as a factor graph, integrating GPS, IMU, and RGB-D observations through robust geometrical constraints that exploit vineyard structure. An efficient perception pipeline based on instance segmentation and tracking, combined with a clustering filter for outlier rejection and pose refinement, enables accurate landmark detection using low-cost sensors and onboard computation. To validate the pipeline, we present a multi-season dataset for trunk and pole segmentation and tracking. Extensive field experiments conducted across diverse seasons demonstrate the robustness and accuracy of the proposed approach, highlighting its suitability for long-term autonomous operation in agricultural environments.

Furthermore, we formulate a joint multi-view Sim(3) optimization that enforces consistent alignment across selected views, substantially improving pose estimation accuracy. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数字孪生系统在机器人操作领域面临三大挑战：缺乏统一模型、复杂动态交互建模困难、以及现实到仿真的差距（real-to-sim gap），这些问题限制了模型预测控制等下游应用的有效性。

Method: 提出GaussTwin系统：1) 结合位置动力学（position-based dynamics）与离散Cosserat杆模型实现物理仿真；2) 采用Gaussian splatting实现高效渲染和视觉校正；3) 将Gaussians锚定到物理图元上，通过光度误差和分割掩码驱动的SE(3)更新，实现稳定的预测-校正循环并保持物理保真度。

Result: 在仿真环境和Franka Research 3机器人平台上的实验表明：1) 与形状匹配和刚性基线相比，GaussTwin在跟踪精度和鲁棒性方面表现更优；2) 成功支持了基于推动的规划等下游任务；3) 实现了实时性能。

Conclusion: GaussTwin是迈向统一、具有物理意义的数字孪生系统的重要一步，能够有效支持闭环机器人交互和学习任务，为机器人操作中的数字孪生应用提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Digital twins promise to enhance robotic manipulation by maintaining a consistent link between real-world perception and simulation. However, most existing systems struggle with the lack of a unified model, complex dynamic interactions, and the real-to-sim gap, which limits downstream applications such as model predictive control. Thus, we propose GaussTwin, a real-time digital twin that combines position-based dynamics with discrete Cosserat rod formulations for physically grounded simulation, and Gaussian splatting for efficient rendering and visual correction. By anchoring Gaussians to physical primitives and enforcing coherent SE(3) updates driven by photometric error and segmentation masks, GaussTwin achieves stable prediction-correction while preserving physical fidelity. Through experiments in both simulation and on a Franka Research 3 platform, we show that GaussTwin consistently improves tracking accuracy and robustness compared to shape-matching and rigid-only baselines, while also enabling downstream tasks such as push-based planning. These results highlight GaussTwin as a step toward unified, physically meaningful digital twins that can support closed-loop robotic interaction and learning.

### [121] [SPIRIT: Perceptive Shared Autonomy for Robust Robotic Manipulation under Deep Learning Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05111)
*Jongseok Lee,Ribin Balachandran,Harsimran Singh,Jianxiang Feng,Hrishik Mishra,Marco De Stefano,Rudolph Triebel,Alin Albu-Schaeffer,Konstantin Kondak*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习在机器人感知领域取得了显著进展，但其鲁棒性有限且缺乏可解释性，阻碍了在安全关键应用中的可靠部署。

Method: 提出感知共享自主性概念，利用深度学习感知的不确定性估计调节自主级别。关键技术是基于神经正切核（NTK）的不确定性感知深度学习点云配准方法，实现置信度高时的半自主操作与不确定性增加时的触觉遥操作之间的平滑过渡。

Result: 通过15名参与者的用户研究和模拟工业场景实现，在挑战性空中操作任务上验证了该方法。系统SPIRIT在深度学习感知失效的情况下仍能实现可靠的机器人操作，同时提升了操作性能和系统可靠性，并入选某重要工业创新奖决赛。

Conclusion: 感知共享自主性框架成功实现了高性能但不透明的深度学习方法在机器人系统中的安全集成，在保持高操作性能的同时确保了系统鲁棒性和可靠性。

Abstract: Deep learning (DL) has enabled impressive advances in robotic perception, yet its limited robustness and lack of interpretability hinder reliable deployment in safety critical applications. We propose a concept termed perceptive shared autonomy, in which uncertainty estimates from DL based perception are used to regulate the level of autonomy. Specifically, when the robot's perception is confident, semi-autonomous manipulation is enabled to improve performance; when uncertainty increases, control transitions to haptic teleoperation for maintaining robustness. In this way, high-performing but uninterpretable DL methods can be integrated safely into robotic systems. A key technical enabler is an uncertainty aware DL based point cloud registration approach based on the so called Neural Tangent Kernels (NTK). We evaluate perceptive shared autonomy on challenging aerial manipulation tasks through a user study of 15 participants and realization of mock-up industrial scenarios, demonstrating reliable robotic manipulation despite failures in DL based perception. The resulting system, named SPIRIT, improves both manipulation performance and system reliability. SPIRIT was selected as a finalist of a major industrial innovation award.

### [122] [SeedPolicy: Horizon Scaling via Self-Evolving Diffusion Policy for Robot Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05117)
*Youqiang Gui,Yuxuan Zhou,Shen Cheng,Xinyang Yuan,Haoqiang Fan,Peng Cheng,Shuaicheng Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了SEGA模块和SeedPolicy方法，解决了Diffusion Policy在长时域操作中的性能下降问题，在RoboTwin 2.0基准测试上相比DP平均提升36.8%-169%，且参数量比RDT等大规模模型少1-2个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模仿学习方法Diffusion Policy虽然能够建模多模态专家行为，但随着观测时域增加会出现性能下降，限制了其在长时域机器人操作任务中的应用。

Method: 提出Self-Evolving Gated Attention (SEGA)时序模块，通过门控注意力机制维护时间演化的潜在状态，实现高效的循环更新，将长时域观测压缩为固定大小表示并过滤无关时序信息。将SEGA集成到Diffusion Policy中形成Self-Evolving Diffusion Policy (SeedPolicy)。

Result: 在RoboTwin 2.0基准的50个操作任务上，SeedPolicy显著优于DP和其他IL基线。平均而言，相比DP在干净环境中提升36.8%，在随机化挑战环境中提升169%。与拥有12亿参数的RDT等视觉-语言-动作模型相比，SeedPolicy在参数量少1-2个数量级的情况下实现了具有竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: SeedPolicy成功解决了长时域机器人操作中的时序建模瓶颈问题，以极高的参数效率实现了最先进的模仿学习性能，证明了该方法在长时域操作任务中的有效性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Imitation Learning (IL) enables robots to acquire manipulation skills from expert demonstrations. Diffusion Policy (DP) models multi-modal expert behaviors but suffers performance degradation as observation horizons increase, limiting long-horizon manipulation. We propose Self-Evolving Gated Attention (SEGA), a temporal module that maintains a time-evolving latent state via gated attention, enabling efficient recurrent updates that compress long-horizon observations into a fixed-size representation while filtering irrelevant temporal information. Integrating SEGA into DP yields Self-Evolving Diffusion Policy (SeedPolicy), which resolves the temporal modeling bottleneck and enables scalable horizon extension with moderate overhead. On the RoboTwin 2.0 benchmark with 50 manipulation tasks, SeedPolicy outperforms DP and other IL baselines. Averaged across both CNN and Transformer backbones, SeedPolicy achieves 36.8% relative improvement in clean settings and 169% relative improvement in randomized challenging settings over the DP. Compared to vision-language-action models such as RDT with 1.2B parameters, SeedPolicy achieves competitive performance with one to two orders of magnitude fewer parameters, demonstrating strong efficiency and scalability. These results establish SeedPolicy as a state-of-the-art imitation learning method for long-horizon robotic manipulation. Code is available at: https://github.com/Youqiang-Gui/SeedPolicy.

### [123] [Lifelong Language-Conditioned Robotic Manipulation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05160)
*Xudong Wang,Zebin Han,Zhiyu Liu,Gan Li,Jiahua Dong,Baichen Liu,Lianqing Liu,Zhi Han*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了SkillsCrafter框架，用于解决语言条件操作智能体在顺序学习新技能时的灾难性遗忘问题。通过操作技能适应和技能专业化聚合两种方法，实现了持续学习新技能的同时保留旧技能知识，显著提升了动态场景下的实用性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统语言条件操作智能体在顺序适应新操作技能时会导致旧技能的灾难性遗忘，严重限制了其在动态场景中的实际部署能力。现有方法难以在学习新技能的同时有效保留已掌握的技能知识。

Method: 提出了SkillsCrafter框架，包含两个核心方法：(1)操作技能适应，通过保留旧技能知识并继承新旧技能间的共享知识来促进新技能学习；(2)对多样化技能指令进行奇异值分解(SVD)获取公共技能语义子空间投影矩阵，记录技能的本质语义空间；(3)技能专业化聚合，通过计算技能语义子空间中的技能间相似度，聚合已学习的技能知识以处理新技能或未知技能。

Result: 广泛的实验表明，SkillsCrafter在持续学习多个操作技能任务中表现出色，有效减少了灾难性遗忘现象，同时在新技能学习和未知技能泛化方面展现了优越性能。

Conclusion: SkillsCrafter成功解决了语言条件操作智能体持续学习中的灾难性遗忘问题，通过技能知识保留、语义子空间建模和知识聚合机制，实现了无遗忘和强泛化的机器人操作能力，为动态场景下的实际应用提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Traditional language-conditioned manipulation agent sequential adaptation to new manipulation skills leads to catastrophic forgetting of old skills, limiting dynamic scene practical deployment. In this paper, we propose SkillsCrafter, a novel robotic manipulation framework designed to continually learn multiple skills while reducing catastrophic forgetting of old skills. Specifically, we propose a Manipulation Skills Adaptation to retain the old skills knowledge while inheriting the shared knowledge between new and old skills to facilitate learning of new skills. Meanwhile, we perform the singular value decomposition on the diverse skill instructions to obtain common skill semantic subspace projection matrices, thereby recording the essential semantic space of skills. To achieve forget-less and generalization manipulation, we propose a Skills Specialization Aggregation to compute inter-skills similarity in skill semantic subspaces, achieving aggregation of the previously learned skill knowledge for any new or unknown skill. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness and superiority of our proposed SkillsCrafter.

### [124] [Critic in the Loop: A Tri-System VLA Framework for Robust Long-Horizon Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05185)
*Pengfei Yi,Yingjie Ma,Wenjiang Xu,Yanan Hao,Shuai Gan,Wanting Li,Shanlin Zhong*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出Critic in the Loop框架，通过仿生三系统架构（VLM大脑+VLA小脑+视觉评判器）动态调度高层推理与低层执行，在保持实时响应的同时实现复杂长周期任务的鲁棒操控，达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法存在权衡困境：视觉语言模型(VLM)擅长高层语义规划但推理延迟高，无法实时执行；快速视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型响应快但缺乏处理复杂长周期任务的语义深度。如何平衡高层语义推理与低层反应控制仍是视觉机器人操控的核心挑战。

Method: 提出仿生三系统架构：1)VLM大脑负责全局推理；2)VLA小脑负责反应式执行；3)轻量级视觉评判器持续监控工作空间，动态路由控制权限。评判器检测执行异常（如任务停滞或失败）时触发VLM重规划，日常子任务由VLA维持快速闭环执行。同时集成类人规则以直觉性地打破无限重试循环。

Result: 在具有挑战性的长周期操控基准测试上进行了全面实验，该方法实现了最先进(SOTA)性能。视觉引导调度显著减少了昂贵的VLM查询次数，同时大幅提升了系统在分布外(OOD)场景中的鲁棒性和自主性。

Conclusion: Critic in the Loop框架成功弥合了高层语义推理与低层反应控制之间的差距，通过动态VLM-Expert调度机制，在最小化VLM调用的同时实现了复杂任务的鲁棒执行，为视觉机器人操控提供了一种有效的层次化解决方案。

Abstract: Balancing high-level semantic reasoning with low-level reactive control remains a core challenge in visual robotic manipulation. While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) excel at cognitive planning, their inference latency precludes real-time execution. Conversely, fast Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models often lack the semantic depth required for complex, long-horizon tasks. To bridge this gap, we introduce Critic in the Loop, an adaptive hierarchical framework driven by dynamic VLM-Expert scheduling. At its core is a bionic Tri-System architecture comprising a VLM brain for global reasoning, a VLA cerebellum for reactive execution, and a lightweight visual Critic. By continuously monitoring the workspace, the Critic dynamically routes control authority. It sustains rapid closed-loop execution via the VLA for routine subtasks, and adaptively triggers the VLM for replanning upon detecting execution anomalies such as task stagnation or failures. Furthermore, our architecture seamlessly integrates human-inspired rules to intuitively break infinite retry loops. This visually-grounded scheduling minimizes expensive VLM queries, while substantially enhancing system robustness and autonomy in out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios. Comprehensive experiments on challenging, long-horizon manipulation benchmarks reveal that our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance.

### [126] [Curve-Induced Dynamical Systems on Riemannian Manifolds and Lie Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05268)
*Saray Bakker,Martin Schonger,Tobias Löw,Javier Alonso-Mora,Sylvain Calinon*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了CDSM框架，用于在黎曼流形和李群上直接构建动力系统，通过在流形上构造名义曲线并结合切向和法向分量生成运动，实现了安全、可适应且可解释的机器人行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 家庭环境中的机器人部署需要安全、可适应且可解释的行为，这些行为需尊重任务的几何结构（如SE(3)上的位姿或SPD矩阵表示的刚度/阻尼矩阵）。现有基于动力系统的方法需要在流形和李群上直接构建系统以保证稳定性和收敛性。

Method: 提出CDSM（Curve-induced Dynamical systems on Smooth Manifolds）框架：1）在流形上构造名义曲线；2）生成动力系统，包含驱动沿曲线运动的切向分量和将状态吸引向曲线的法向分量；3）提供稳定性分析。该方法支持在黎曼流形和李群上实时构建动力系统。

Result: 在S2基准测试中，CDSM相比最先进方法展现出更高的轨迹精度、更小的路径偏差以及更快的生成和查询时间。在实际机器人应用中成功验证：机械臂上实时适应SE(3)位姿和SPD(n)阻尼矩阵，以及移动操作平台上的应用。

Conclusion: CDSM框架成功实现了在黎曼流形和李群上直接构建动力系统，提供了稳定性保证，在准确性和计算效率上优于现有方法，并在实际机器人系统中验证了其实用性，为家庭环境中机器人行为生成提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Deploying robots in household environments requires safe, adaptable, and interpretable behaviors that respect the geometric structure of tasks. Often represented on Lie groups and Riemannian manifolds, this includes poses on SE(3) or symmetric positive definite matrices encoding stiffness or damping matrices. In this context, dynamical system-based approaches offer a natural framework for generating such behavior, providing stability and convergence while remaining responsive to changes in the environment. We introduce Curve-induced Dynamical systems on Smooth Manifolds (CDSM), a real-time framework for constructing dynamical systems directly on Riemannian manifolds and Lie groups. The proposed approach constructs a nominal curve on the manifold, and generates a dynamical system which combines a tangential component that drives motion along the curve and a normal component that attracts the state toward the curve. We provide a stability analysis of the resulting dynamical system and validate the method quantitatively. On an S2 benchmark, CDSM demonstrates improved trajectory accuracy, reduced path deviation, and faster generation and query times compared to state-of-the-art methods. Finally, we demonstrate the practical applicability of the framework on both a robotic manipulator, where poses on SE(3) and damping matrices on SPD(n) are adapted online, and a mobile manipulator.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言条件操作层次化策略存在关键问题：高层规划器在生成子目标时未考虑低层控制器的实际能力限制，导致策略经常失败。现有解决方案（如中间模块或共享表示）仍受限于固定的离线数据集，无法有效弥合规划器与控制器之间的差距。

Method: 提出HD-ExpIt框架，将训练组织成一个自我强化循环：(1)利用基于扩散的规划自主发现成功行为；(2)将这些成功行为蒸馏回层次化策略。该循环使两个组件能够共同改进，同时隐式地将规划器建立在控制器的实际能力基础上，无需显式的代理模型。

Result: HD-ExpIt显著提升了仅使用离线数据训练的层次化策略性能，在长视野CALVIN基准测试中，在从头训练的方法中达到了最先进的性能。

Conclusion: 通过环境反馈的迭代微调机制，HD-ExpIt成功解决了层次化策略中规划器与控制器能力不匹配的核心问题，证明了自主行为发现与策略蒸馏相结合的有效性，为离线数据驱动的层次化策略学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Hierarchical policies for language-conditioned manipulation decompose tasks into subgoals, where a high-level planner guides a low-level controller. However, these hierarchical agents often fail because the planner generates subgoals without considering the actual limitations of the controller. Existing solutions attempt to bridge this gap via intermediate modules or shared representations, but they remain limited by their reliance on fixed offline datasets. We propose HD-ExpIt, a framework for iterative fine-tuning of hierarchical diffusion policies via environment feedback. HD-ExpIt organizes training into a self-reinforcing cycle: it utilizes diffusion-based planning to autonomously discover successful behaviors, which are then distilled back into the hierarchical policy. This loop enables both components to improve while implicitly grounding the planner in the controller's actual capabilities without requiring explicit proxy models. Empirically, HD-ExpIt significantly improves hierarchical policies trained solely on offline data, achieving state-of-the-art performance on the long-horizon CALVIN benchmark among methods trained from scratch.

### [129] [Latent Policy Steering through One-Step Flow Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05296)
*Hokyun Im,Andrey Kolobov,Jianlong Fu,Youngwoon Lee*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了潜在策略引导（LPS）方法，通过在潜在动作空间中进行端到端优化，解决了离线强化学习中回报最大化与行为约束之间的脆弱权衡问题，在多个基准和真实机器人任务上达到了最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线强化学习中的性能往往受限于回报最大化与行为约束之间的脆弱权衡：前者可能导致策略偏离数据集支持范围，后者则需要敏感的超参数调优。现有的潜在引导方法通过间接蒸馏学习潜在空间评论家来近似动作价值，但这会丢失信息并阻碍收敛。

Method: 提出潜在策略引导（LPS）方法，通过可微的单步MeanFlow策略，将原始动作空间的Q梯度反向传播到潜在动作空间的行动者来更新策略。该方法消除了代理潜在评论家，使用原始动作空间评论家引导端到端的潜在空间优化，同时单步MeanFlow策略作为行为约束的生成先验，实现了原始动作空间优化与潜在空间优化之间的解耦。

Result: 在OGBench基准测试和真实世界机器人任务上，LPS达到了最先进性能，并且持续优于行为克隆和强潜在引导基线方法。该方法具有鲁棒性，开箱即用且只需最小化的超参数调优。

Conclusion: LPS通过解耦原始动作空间优化与潜在空间优化，成功解决了离线强化学习中的关键挑战，为机器人离线学习提供了一种高效、鲁棒且易于使用的解决方案。

Abstract: Offline reinforcement learning (RL) allows robots to learn from offline datasets without risky exploration. Yet, offline RL's performance often hinges on a brittle trade-off between (1) return maximization, which can push policies outside the dataset support, and (2) behavioral constraints, which typically require sensitive hyperparameter tuning. Latent steering offers a structural way to stay within the dataset support during RL, but existing offline adaptations commonly approximate action values using latent-space critics learned via indirect distillation, which can lose information and hinder convergence. We propose Latent Policy Steering (LPS), which enables high-fidelity latent policy improvement by backpropagating original-action-space Q-gradients through a differentiable one-step MeanFlow policy to update a latent-action-space actor. By eliminating proxy latent critics, LPS allows an original-action-space critic to guide end-to-end latent-space optimization, while the one-step MeanFlow policy serves as a behavior-constrained generative prior. This decoupling yields a robust method that works out-of-the-box with minimal tuning. Across OGBench and real-world robotic tasks, LPS achieves state-of-the-art performance and consistently outperforms behavioral cloning and strong latent steering baselines.

</details>


### [130] [Constraint-Free Static Modeling of Continuum Parallel Robot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05309)
*Lingxiao Xun,Matyas Diezinger,Azad Artinian,Guillaume Laurent,Brahim Tamadazte*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种几何精确、无约束的连续体并联机器人静态建模方法，通过运动学嵌入消除连接约束，在几何非线性大变形条件下实现了高效准确的静力学求解，并通过实验验证了模型的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续体并联机器人在刚性-连续体连接处存在显式运动学约束，传统的基于约束的公式化方法引入额外代数变量，导致数值求解和下游控制复杂化。为了解决这一问题，本文旨在开发一种无约束的静态模型。

Method: 通过运动学嵌入消除连接约束，将每根杆件在SE(3)流形上用节点位姿离散化，采用线性应变参数化重建单元应变场。利用四阶Magnus近似建立单元端部位姿与应变之间的显式几何一致映射。基于总势能和虚功推导装配-ready残差和显式牛顿切线，在乘积流形上使用黎曼牛顿迭代求解非线性平衡方程。

Result: 在三伺服电机、六杆原型机上进行的实验表明，所提出的模型在无负载运动和外部负载情况下，仿真结果与测量数据均呈现良好一致性，验证了模型的有效性。

Conclusion: 该几何精确、无约束的静态模型成功解决了连续体并联机器人的静力学建模难题，在保持几何非线性大变形大转动有效性的同时，简化了问题求解，为连续体并联机器人的分析和控制提供了有效的理论工具。

Abstract: Continuum parallel robots (CPR) combine rigid actuation mechanisms with multiple elastic rods in a closed-loop topology, making forward statics challenging when rigid--continuum junctions are enforced by explicit kinematic constraints. Such constraint-based formulations typically introduce additional algebraic variables and complicate both numerical solution and downstream control. This paper presents a geometric exact, configuration-based and constraint-free static model of CPR that remains valid under geometrically nonlinear, large-deformation and large-rotation conditions. Connectivity constraints are eliminated by kinematic embedding, yielding a reduced unconstrained problem. Each rod of CPR is discretized by nodal poses on SE(3), while the element-wise strain field is reconstructed through a linear strain parameterization. A fourth-order Magnus approximation yields an explicit and geometrically consistent mapping between element end poses and the strain. Rigid attachments at the motor-driven base and the end-effector platforms are handled through kinematic embeddings. Based on total potential energy and virtual work, we derive assembly-ready residuals and explicit Newton tangents, and solve the resulting nonlinear equilibrium equations using a Riemannian Newton iteration on the product manifold. Experiments on a three-servomotor, six-rod prototype validate the model by showing good agreement between simulation and measurements for both unloaded motions and externally loaded cases.

*Sizhe Yang,Yiman Xie,Zhixuan Liang,Yang Tian,Jia Zeng,Dahua Lin,Jiangmiao Pang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了UltraDexGrasp框架，用于双手机器人的通用灵巧抓取，构建了包含2000万帧的大规模多策略数据集UltraDexGrasp-20M，并开发了基于点云输入的抓取策略，在真实世界零样本迁移中达到81.2%的成功率。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: UltraDexGrasp框架有效解决了双手机器人灵巧抓取的数据瓶颈和策略学习问题，生成的数据集和抓取策略在真实世界表现出优异的泛化能力。研究开源了数据生成管道，为未来双手机器人抓取研究提供了重要资源。

Abstract: Grasping is a fundamental capability for robots to interact with the physical world. Humans, equipped with two hands, autonomously select appropriate grasp strategies based on the shape, size, and weight of objects, enabling robust grasping and subsequent manipulation. In contrast, current robotic grasping remains limited, particularly in multi-strategy settings. Although substantial efforts have targeted parallel-gripper and single-hand grasping, dexterous grasping for bimanual robots remains underexplored, with data being a primary bottleneck. Achieving physically plausible and geometrically conforming grasps that can withstand external wrenches poses significant challenges. To address these issues, we introduce UltraDexGrasp, a framework for universal dexterous grasping with bimanual robots. The proposed data-generation pipeline integrates optimization-based grasp synthesis with planning-based demonstration generation, yielding high-quality and diverse trajectories across multiple grasp strategies. With this framework, we curate UltraDexGrasp-20M, a large-scale, multi-strategy grasp dataset comprising 20 million frames across 1,000 objects. Based on UltraDexGrasp-20M, we further develop a simple yet effective grasp policy that takes point clouds as input, aggregates scene features via unidirectional attention, and predicts control commands. Trained exclusively on synthetic data, the policy achieves robust zero-shot sim-to-real transfer and consistently succeeds on novel objects with varied shapes, sizes, and weights, attaining an average success rate of 81.2% in real-world universal dexterous grasping. We develop a low-dimensional, differentiable Cosserat-rod model of the electrode array coupled with frictional contact and pseudo-dynamics regularization to ensure continuous stick-slip transitions. Patient-specific cochlear anatomy is reconstructed from CT imaging and encoded via an analytic parametrization of the scala-tympani lumen, enabling efficient and differentiable contact queries through closest-point projection. Abstract: The deployment of humanoid robots for dexterous manipulation in unstructured environments remains challenging due to perceptual limitations that constrain the effective workspace.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放世界导航要求机器人在复杂日常环境中做出决策并适应灵活的任务需求。现有方法存在明显局限：传统导航方法依赖密集3D重建和人工设计的目标度量，泛化能力受限；近期视觉-语言导航（VLN）和视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型虽支持端到端策略，但通常需要交互式训练、大规模数据收集或针对特定任务进行微调。

Method: 本文将导航建模为稀疏子目标识别与到达问题。核心洞察是：为高层语义先验提供视觉锚定目标可实现高效的 goal-conditioned 导航。基于此，选择导航前沿（navigation frontiers）作为语义锚点，提出OpenFrontier框架。该框架无需训练，无缝集成多种视觉-语言先验模型，系统设计轻量化，无需密集3D建图、策略训练或模型微调。

Result: 在多个导航基准测试上评估OpenFrontier，展示了强大的零样本性能。同时在真实移动机器人上实现了有效部署，验证了其实用性。

Conclusion: OpenFrontier提供了一种高效、实用的开放世界导航解决方案，通过稀疏子目标识别和视觉锚定机制，避免了传统方法对密集重建和训练的依赖，实现了良好的泛化性能和实际部署能力。

Abstract: Open-world navigation requires robots to make decisions in complex everyday environments while adapting to flexible task requirements. Conventional navigation approaches often rely on dense 3D reconstruction and hand-crafted goal metrics, which limits their generalization across tasks and environments. Recent advances in vision--language navigation (VLN) and vision--language--action (VLA) models enable end-to-end policies conditioned on natural language, but typically require interactive training, large-scale data collection, or task-specific fine-tuning with a mobile agent. We formulate navigation as a sparse subgoal identification and reaching problem and observe that providing visual anchoring targets for high-level semantic priors enables highly efficient goal-conditioned navigation. Based on this insight, we select navigation frontiers as semantic anchors and propose OpenFrontier, a training-free navigation framework that seamlessly integrates diverse vision--language prior models. OpenFrontier enables efficient navigation with a lightweight system design, without dense 3D mapping, policy training, or model fine-tuning. We evaluate OpenFrontier across multiple navigation benchmarks and demonstrate strong zero-shot performance, as well as effective real-world deployment on a mobile robot.

Method: 提出MPPI-DK控制器：使用深度Koopman算子(DKO)从交互数据中学习线性动力学模型，替代原始非线性动力学进行轨迹传播；线性模型使轨迹推演和采样更高效，无需解析系统模型。

Abstract: This paper presents an efficient model predictive path integral (MPPI) control framework for systems with complex nonlinear dynamics. The DKO dynamics are learned directly from interaction data, eliminating the need for analytical system models. The resulting controller, termed MPPI-DK, is evaluated in simulation on pendulum balancing and surface vehicle navigation tasks, and validated on hardware through reference-tracking experiments on a quadruped robot. Experimental results demonstrate that MPPI-DK achieves control performance close to MPPI with true dynamics while substantially reducing computational cost, enabling efficient real-time control on robotic platforms.

### [136] [Loop Closure via Maximal Cliques in 3D LiDAR-Based SLAM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05397)
*Javier Laserna,Saurabh Gupta,Oscar Martinez Mozos,Cyrill Stachniss,Pablo San Segundo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CliReg的确定性算法，用于3D LiDAR SLAM中的回环检测验证，通过在特征对应的兼容性图上进行最大团搜索来替代RANSAC，提高了在噪声和异常值存在下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在3D LiDAR SLAM中，可靠的回环检测面临传感器噪声、环境歧义性和视点变化等挑战。传统方法使用RANSAC进行几何模型拟合，但在异常值存在时可能失败，导致地图不一致。因此需要一种更鲁棒的回环验证方法。

Method: 提出CliReg算法，将回环验证问题建模为在特征对应的兼容性图上进行最大团搜索问题，避免了RANSAC的随机采样过程。该方法集成到实时流程中，采用二进制3D描述符和基于汉明距离嵌入的二叉搜索树匹配。此外，还验证了该方法在2D投影地图上的通用性。

Result: 在多个真实世界数据集和不同LiDAR传感器上的评估表明，该方法在位姿误差和回环可靠性方面均优于RANSAC，尤其在稀疏或歧义环境下表现更佳。在2D投影地图上的实验也证实了其跨空间域的通用性。

Conclusion: CliReg提供了一种鲁棒且高效的回环检测替代方案，能够有效处理噪声和异常值，避免地图不一致性，适用于多种LiDAR传感器和空间域。

Abstract: Reliable loop closure detection remains a critical challenge in 3D LiDAR-based SLAM, especially under sensor noise, environmental ambiguity, and viewpoint variation conditions. RANSAC is often used in the context of loop closures for geometric model fitting in the presence of outliers. However, this approach may fail, leading to map inconsistency. We introduce a novel deterministic algorithm, CliReg, for loop closure validation that replaces RANSAC verification with a maximal clique search over a compatibility graph of feature correspondences. This formulation avoids random sampling and increases robustness in the presence of noise and outliers. We integrated our approach into a real- time pipeline employing binary 3D descriptors and a Hamming distance embedding binary search tree-based matching. We evaluated it on multiple real-world datasets featuring diverse LiDAR sensors. The results demonstrate that our proposed technique consistently achieves a lower pose error and more reliable loop closures than RANSAC, especially in sparse or ambiguous conditions. Additional experiments on 2D projection-based maps confirm its generality across spatial domains, making our approach a robust and efficient alternative for loop closure detection.

Abstract: Contact-rich micromanipulation in microfluidic flow is challenging because small disturbances can break pushing contact and induce large lateral drift. We propose a hybrid controller that augments a nominal MPC with a learned residual policy trained by SAC. The policy outputs a bounded 2D velocity correction that is contact-gated, so residual actions are applied only during robot--cell contact, preserving reliable approach behavior and stabilizing learning. All methods share the same actuation interface and speed envelope for fair comparisons. Experiments show improved robustness and tracking accuracy over pure MPC and PID under nonstationary flow, with generalization from a clover training curve to unseen circle and square trajectories. A residual-bound sweep identifies an intermediate correction limit as the best trade-off, which we use in all benchmarks.

### [140] [Observing and Controlling Features in Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05487)
*Hugo Buurmeijer,Carmen Amo Alonso,Aiden Swann,Marco Pavone*

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action Models (VLAs) have shown remarkable progress towards embodied intelligence. While their architecture partially resembles that of Large Language Models (LLMs), VLAs exhibit higher complexity due to their multi-modal inputs/outputs and often hybrid nature of transformer and diffusion heads. This is part of the reason why insights from mechanistic interpretability in LLMs, which explain how the internal model representations relate to their output behavior, do not trivially transfer to VLA counterparts. In this work, we propose to close this gap by introducing and analyzing two main concepts: feature-observability and feature-controllability. In particular, we first study features that are linearly encoded in representation space, and show how they can be observed by means of a linear classifier. Then, we use a minimal linear intervention grounded in optimal control to accurately place internal representations and steer the VLA's output towards a desired region. Our results show that targeted, lightweight interventions can reliably steer a robot's behavior while preserving closed-loop capabilities. We demonstrate on different VLA architectures ($π_{0.5}$ and OpenVLA) through simulation experiments that VLAs possess interpretable internal structure amenable to online adaptation without fine-tuning, enabling real-time alignment with user preferences and task requirements.

### [141] [cuRoboV2: Dynamics-Aware Motion Generation with Depth-Fused Distance Fields for High-DoF Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05493)
*Balakumar Sundaralingam,Adithyavairavan Murali,Stan Birchfield*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出cuRoboV2统一框架，通过GPU加速实现从机械臂到高自由度人形机器人的安全、可行、反应式运动生成，在碰撞检测、轨迹优化和运动学求解方面显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人运动生成方法存在碎片化问题：快速规划器生成物理上不可执行的轨迹，反应式控制器难以处理高精度感知，现有求解器无法处理高自由度系统。需要统一的解决方案来确保运动的安全性、可行性和反应性。

Method: 提出三项核心创新：(1)B样条轨迹优化，强制执行平滑性和扭矩限制；(2)GPU原生TSDF/ESDF感知管线，生成覆盖整个工作空间的密集符号距离场；(3)可扩展的GPU原生全身计算，包括拓扑感知运动学、可微分逆动力学和map-reduce自碰撞检测。采用重新设计的代码架构以支持LLM编码助手协作开发。

Conclusion: cuRoboV2提供了统一的、动态感知的运动生成技术栈，能够从单臂机械臂扩展到完整的人形机器人，解决了现有方法在高自由度系统和高质量感知方面的局限性，同时展示了良好结构的机器人代码可以促进人机协作开发。

Abstract: Effective robot autonomy requires motion generation that is safe, feasible, and reactive. Current methods are fragmented: fast planners output physically unexecutable trajectories, reactive controllers struggle with high-fidelity perception, and existing solvers fail on high-DoF systems. We present cuRoboV2, a unified framework with three key innovations: (1) B-spline trajectory optimization that enforces smoothness and torque limits; (2) a GPU-native TSDF/ESDF perception pipeline that generates dense signed distance fields covering the full workspace, unlike existing methods that only provide distances within sparsely allocated blocks, up to 10x faster and in 8x less memory than the state-of-the-art at manipulation scale, with up to 99% collision recall; and (3) scalable GPU-native whole-body computation, namely topology-aware kinematics, differentiable inverse dynamics, and map-reduce self-collision, that achieves up to 61x speedup while also extending to high-DoF humanoids (where previous GPU implementations fail). On benchmarks, cuRoboV2 achieves 99.7% success under 3kg payload (where baselines achieve only 72--77%), 99.6% collision-free IK on a 48-DoF humanoid (where prior methods fail entirely), and 89.5% retargeting constraint satisfaction (vs. 61% for PyRoki); these collision-free motions yield locomotion policies with 21% lower tracking error than PyRoki and 12x lower cross-seed variance than mink. A ground-up codebase redesign for discoverability enabled LLM coding assistants to author up to 73% of new modules, including hand-optimized CUDA kernels, demonstrating that well-structured robotics code can unlock productive human--LLM collaboration. Together, these advances provide a unified, dynamics-aware motion generation stack that scales from single-arm manipulators to full humanoids.

*Lizhi Yang,Ryan M. Bena,Meg Wilkinson,Gilbert Bahati,Andy Navarro Brenes,Ryan K. Cosner,Aaron D. Ames*

Method: 提出Safe-SAGE统一框架，主要包括：(1) 多传感器点云与视觉实例分割融合，结合持久目标跟踪维持相机视场外的语义信息；(2) 设计泊松安全函数(PSF)并结合拉普拉斯引导场进行调制；(3) 构建多层安全滤波器，包含模型预测控制层和控制障碍函数层，两层均利用PSF和引导场通量调制，为不同障碍物引入差异化的保守性和多智能体通行规范。

Result: 该框架能够使足式机器人在语义丰富、动态变化的环境中导航，同时根据障碍物的语义特征实现上下文相关的安全边界，并保持严格的安全保证。

Conclusion: Safe-SAGE成功弥合了高层语义理解与底层安全关键控制之间的鸿沟，通过语义自适应引导实现了对障碍物的差异化安全处理，为复杂动态环境下的机器人导航提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Traditional safety-critical control methods, such as control barrier functions, suffer from semantic blindness, exhibiting the same behavior around obstacles regardless of contextual significance. This limitation leads to the uniform treatment of all obstacles, despite their differing semantic meanings. We present Safe-SAGE (Social-Semantic Adaptive Guidance for Safe Engagement), a unified framework that bridges the gap between high-level semantic understanding and low-level safety-critical control through a Poisson safety function (PSF) modulated using a Laplace guidance field. Our approach perceives the environment by fusing multi-sensor point clouds with vision-based instance segmentation and persistent object tracking to maintain up-to-date semantics beyond the camera's field of view. A multi-layer safety filter is then used to modulate system inputs to achieve safe navigation using this semantic understanding of the environment. This safety filter consists of both a model predictive control layer and a control barrier function layer. Both layers utilize the PSF and flux modulation of the guidance field to introduce varying levels of conservatism and multi-agent passing norms for different obstacles in the environment. Our framework enables legged robots to navigate semantically rich, dynamic environments with context-dependent safety margins while maintaining rigorous safety guarantees.

</details>


### [143] [RoboPocket: Improve Robot Policies Instantly with Your Phone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05504)
*Junjie Fang,Wendi Chen,Han Xue,Fangyuan Zhou,Tian Le,Yi Wang,Yuting Zhang,Jun Lv,Chuan Wen,Cewu Lu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了RoboPocket，一种基于智能手机的便携式系统，通过增强现实(AR)可视化策略预测轨迹，实现了无需物理机器人的即时策略迭代，将数据效率相比离线方法提升了两倍。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现模仿学习的数据收集存在效率瓶颈：手持界面虽然可扩展但采用开环方式，操作者无法感知策略弱点导致数据覆盖效率低；而DAgger等交互式方法虽能解决协变量偏移问题，但依赖物理机器人执行，成本高且难以扩展。研究旨在调和这一权衡，实现既可扩展又高效的数据收集方法。

Method: 提出RoboPocket系统，包含两大核心创新：(1)远程推理框架，利用增强现实(AR)视觉预见可视化策略的预测轨迹，使收集者能主动识别潜在失败并聚焦于策略薄弱区域进行数据收集；(2)异步在线微调管道，持续用新收集数据更新策略，在分钟级别有效闭合学习环路。整个系统仅需消费级智能手机，无需物理机器人。

Result: 实验表明：(1)RoboPocket遵循数据扩展定律；(2)相比离线扩展策略，数据效率提升两倍，突破了长期存在的效率瓶颈；(3)即时迭代循环在分布式环境中将样本效率提升高达2倍，每人仅需少量交互修正。

Conclusion: RoboPocket成功实现了无需物理机器人的即时策略迭代，通过AR反馈闭环有效解决了模仿学习中数据收集效率与可扩展性之间的矛盾，为规模化模仿学习提供了实用且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Scaling imitation learning is fundamentally constrained by the efficiency of data collection. While handheld interfaces have emerged as a scalable solution for in-the-wild data acquisition, they predominantly operate in an open-loop manner: operators blindly collect demonstrations without knowing the underlying policy's weaknesses, leading to inefficient coverage of critical state distributions. Conversely, interactive methods like DAgger effectively address covariate shift but rely on physical robot execution, which is costly and difficult to scale. To reconcile this trade-off, we introduce RoboPocket, a portable system that enables Robot-Free Instant Policy Iteration using single consumer smartphones. Its core innovation is a Remote Inference framework that visualizes the policy's predicted trajectory via Augmented Reality (AR) Visual Foresight. This immersive feedback allows collectors to proactively identify potential failures and focus data collection on the policy's weak regions without requiring a physical robot. Furthermore, we implement an asynchronous Online Finetuning pipeline that continuously updates the policy with incoming data, effectively closing the learning loop in minutes. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RoboPocket adheres to data scaling laws and doubles the data efficiency compared to offline scaling strategies, overcoming their long-standing efficiency bottleneck. Moreover, our instant iteration loop also boosts sample efficiency by up to 2$\times$ in distributed environments a small number of interactive corrections per person. Project page and videos: https://robo-pocket.github.io.

</details>

### [144] [HDLFORGE: A Two-Stage Multi-Agent Framework for Efficient Verilog Code Generation with Adaptive Model Escalation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04646)
*Armin Abdollahi,Saeid Shokoufa,Negin Ashrafi,Mehdi Kamal,Massoud Pedram*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出两阶段框架：Stage A默认使用中等规模LLM的紧凑编码器，Stage B仅在需要时升级到超大规模LLM的强力编码器。升级决策由校准分数引导，该分数基于编译、lint和冒烟测试等低成本诊断。关键创新包括：反例引导的形式化智能体，将有界模型检测追踪转换为可重用的微测试；可移植的升级控制器，无需修改现有Verilog LLM流水线即可封装。

Result: 在VerilogEval Human、VerilogEval V2和RTLLM基准上评估。HDLFORGE-Qwen在VerilogEval Human和V2上分别达到91.2%和91.8%的Pass@1，中位延迟降低约50%，在RTLLM上达到97.2%的Pass@5。相比单阶段系统展现出更优的准确率-延迟权衡。

Conclusion: HDLFORGE通过两阶段升级策略和形式化智能体创新，成功优化了Verilog自动生成的速度-准确性权衡，为硬件描述语言代码生成提供了一种高效、可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: We present HDLFORGE, a two-stage multi-agent framework for automated Verilog generation that optimizes the trade-off between generation speed and accuracy. The system uses a compact coder with a medium-sized LLM by default (Stage A) and escalates to a stronger coder with an ultra-large LLM (Stage B) only when needed, guided by a calibrated score from inexpensive diagnostics including compilation, lint, and smoke tests. A key innovation is a counterexample-guided formal agent that converts bounded-model-checking traces into reusable micro-tests, significantly reducing bug detection time and repair iterations. The portable escalation controller can wrap existing Verilog LLM pipelines without modifying their internals. Evaluated on VerilogEval Human, VerilogEval V2, and RTLLM benchmarks, HDLFORGE demonstrates improved accuracy-latency trade-offs compared to single-stage systems through comprehensive analysis of wall-clock time distributions, escalation thresholds, and agent ablations. On VerilogEval Human and VerilogEval V2, HDLFORGE-Qwen achieves 91.2% and 91.8% Pass@1 with roughly 50% lower median latency, dramatically improving accuracy over other medium-sized models, and 97.2% Pass@5 on RTLLM.

### [145] [Hardware-Software Co-design for 3D-DRAM-based LLM Serving Accelerator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04797)
*Cong Li,Yihan Yin,Chenhao Xue,Zhao Wang,Fujun Bai,Yixin Guo,Xiping Jiang,Qiang Wu,Yuan Xie,Guangyu Sun*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
