Method: 提出Helios混合键合LLM服务加速器，设计了PE内执行流程和PE间通信原语以实现分布式分块注意力执行；提出空间感知的KV缓存分配机制，在最小化PE间数据传输开销的同时平衡注意力工作负载分布。

Result: 与现有GPU/NMP设计相比，Helios实现了3.25倍（几何平均）加速、3.36倍（几何平均）更好的能效，P50/P99 token间时间延迟降低了72%/76%。

Conclusion: Helios成功弥合了LLM服务中KV缓存管理的动态特性与NMP处理引擎间分布式、非均匀内存抽象之间的根本差距，为动态LLM服务工作负载提供了高效的加速方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have been widely deployed for online generative services, where numerous LLM instances jointly handle workloads with fluctuating request arrival rates and variable request lengths. To efficiently execute coexisting compute-intensive and memory-intensive operators, near-memory processing (NMP) based computing paradigm has been extensively proposed. However, existing NMP designs adopt coarse-grained KV cache management and inflexible attention execution flow. Such limitations hinder these proposals from efficiently handling \textit{highly dynamic} LLM serving workloads, limiting their ability to accelerate LLM serving.
  To tackle these problems, we propose Helios, a Hybrid-bonding-based \uline{L}LM \uline{S}erving accelerator. Helios aims to bridge the fundamental gap between the dynamic nature of KV cache management in LLM serving and the distributed, non-uniform memory abstraction among NMP processing engines (PEs). To this end, we design both the intra-PE execution flow and the inter-PE communication primitives for distributed tiled attention execution. We further propose \textit{spatially-aware} KV cache allocation mechanism to balance the attention workload distribution while minimizing the inter-PE data transfer overhead. Compared with existing GPU/NMP designs, Helios achieves 3.25 times (geomean) speedup and 3.36 times (geomean) better energy efficiency, along with up to 72%/76% P50/P99 time-between-tokens degradation.

### [146] [VMXDOTP: A RISC-V Vector ISA Extension for Efficient Microscaling (MX) Format Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04979)
*Max Wipfli,Gamze İslamoğlu,Navaneeth Kunhi Purayil,Angelo Garofalo,Luca Benini*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出VMXDOTP，一种面向RISC-V向量架构的指令集扩展，用于高效执行Microscaling (MX)数据格式的点积运算。在12nm工艺下实现，相比软件模拟实现最高提升7.0倍速度和4.9倍能效，面积开销仅7.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代基于解码器的Transformer模型需要灵活的加速器，MX数据格式虽能减少数据量并保持精度，但其语义（块缩放、多步混合精度操作）与向量执行模型不匹配，导致流水线不规则、计算资源利用率低和性能下降。

Method: 提出VMXDOTP指令集扩展，支持MXFP8和MXFP4输入、FP32和BF16累加以及软件定义的块大小，设计并实现了增强型VPE集群。

Result: 在MX-MatMul上达到97%利用率；在12nm FinFET工艺、1GHz、0.8V下实现125 MXFP8-GFLOPS和250 MXFP4-GFLOPS，能效达843/1632 MXFP8/MXFP4-GFLOPS/W，面积开销仅7.2%；相比软件模拟最高提升7.0倍速度和4.9倍能效；相比现有MX引擎面积效率提升1.4倍，能效提升2.1倍。

Conclusion: VMXDOTP有效解决了MX格式与向量执行的不匹配问题，实现了高利用率、高能效和低面积开销，为现代Transformer模型提供了一种高效的加速方案。

Abstract: Compared to the first generation of deep neural networks, dominated by regular, compute-intensive kernels such as matrix multiplications (MatMuls) and convolutions, modern decoder-based transformers interleave attention, normalization, and data-dependent control flow. This demands flexible accelerators, a requirement met by scalable, highly energy-efficient shared-L1-memory vector processing element (VPE) clusters. Meanwhile, the ever-growing size and bandwidth needs of state-of-the-art models make reduced-precision formats increasingly attractive. Microscaling (MX) data formats, based on block floating-point (BFP) representations, have emerged as a promising solution to reduce data volumes while preserving accuracy. However, MX semantics are poorly aligned with vector execution: block scaling and multi-step mixed-precision operations break the regularity of vector pipelines, leading to underutilized compute resources and performance degradation. To address these challenges, we propose VMXDOTP, a RISC-V Vector (RVV) 1.0 instruction set architecture (ISA) extension for efficient MX dot product execution, supporting MXFP8 and MXFP4 inputs, FP32 and BF16 accumulation, and software-defined block sizes. A VMXDOTP-enhanced VPE cluster achieves up to 97 % utilization on MX-MatMul. Implemented in 12 nm FinFET, it achieves up to 125 MXFP8-GFLOPS and 250 MXFP4-GFLOPS, with 843/1632 MXFP8/MXFP4-GFLOPS/W at 1 GHz, 0.8 V, and only 7.2 % area overhead. Our design yields up to 7.0x speedup and 4.9x energy efficiency with respect to software-emulated MXFP8-MatMul. Compared with prior MX engines, VMXDOTP supports variable block sizes, is up to 1.4x more area-efficient, and delivers up to 2.1x higher energy efficiency.

</details>

In this paper, we investigate how the physical placement of reticles on wafers influences the achievable network topology and the resulting communication performance. Starting from a 2D mesh-like baseline, we propose four reticle placements (Aligned, Interleaved, Rotated, and Contoured) that improve throughput by up to 250%, reduce latency by up to 36%, and decrease energy per transmitted byte by up to 38%.

### [148] [NL2GDS: LLM-aided interface for Open Source Chip Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05489)
*Max Eland,Jeyan Thiyagalingam,Dinesh Pamunuwa,Roshan Weerasekera*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了NL2GDS框架，利用大语言模型（LLM）将自然语言硬件描述自动转换为可综合的RTL代码及完整的GDSII版图，实现了从高层规范到物理实现的自动化流程，并在基准测试中取得了显著的面积、延迟和功耗优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着硬件设计复杂度的不断增长，高层规范与寄存器传输级（RTL）实现之间的鸿沟日益扩大，严重阻碍了快速原型设计和系统设计流程，因此亟需一种能够弥合这一差距的自动化设计方法。

Method: 提出NL2GDS框架，采用模块化流水线架构：首先捕捉非形式化的设计意图，然后利用多个LLM引擎生成硬件描述语言（HDL）代码并进行验证，最后通过开源OpenLane ASIC流程编排自动化的综合与版图生成，实现从自然语言到GDSII布局的完整转换。

Result: 在ISCAS'85和ISCAS'89基准设计上的评估结果表明，与基准设计相比，该框架实现了最高36%的面积缩减、35%的延迟降低以及70%的功耗节省。

Conclusion: NL2GDS展示了利用大语言模型实现硬件设计自动化的巨大潜力，能够有效降低ASIC设计门槛，加速硬件创新进程，为硬件设计民主化提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: The growing complexity of hardware design and the widening gap between high-level specifications and register-transfer level (RTL) implementation hinder rapid prototyping and system design. We introduce NL2GDS (Natural Language to Layout), a novel framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to translate natural language hardware descriptions into synthesizable RTL and complete GDSII layouts via the open-source OpenLane ASIC flow. NL2GDS employs a modular pipeline that captures informal design intent, generates HDL using multiple LLM engines and verifies them, and orchestrates automated synthesis and layout. Evaluations on ISCAS'85 and ISCAS'89 benchmark designs demonstrate up to 36% area reduction, 35% delay reduction, and 70% power savings compared to baseline designs, highlighting its potential to democratize ASIC design and accelerate hardware innovation.

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [149] [AMV-L: Lifecycle-Managed Agent Memory for Tail-Latency Control in Long-Running LLM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04443)
*Emmanuel Bamidele*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出AMV-L框架，通过基于效用评分的价值驱动生命周期管理，解决长运行LLM代理中传统TTL内存管理导致的重尾延迟和吞吐不稳定问题，实现吞吐提升3.1倍、延迟降低4.2倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长运行LLM代理系统多采用基于时间的TTL内存保留策略，但该方法无法限制请求路径上的计算开销。随着保留项累积，检索候选集和向量相似度扫描规模不可预测地增长，导致重尾延迟和吞吐不稳定，难以满足生产环境对可预测性能的需求。

Method: 提出AMV-L（自适应内存价值生命周期）框架，将代理内存视为受管系统资源。核心方法包括：为每个内存项分配持续更新的效用评分，通过价值驱动的提升、降级和驱逐操作维护生命周期分层；检索仅限于有界的、分层感知的候选集，从而将请求路径工作集与总保留内存解耦。

Result: 在相同长运行工作负载下，相比TTL基线，AMV-L吞吐提升3.1倍，中位延迟降低4.2倍（p95降低4.7倍，p99降低4.4倍），超过2秒的请求比例从13.8%降至0.007%。相比LRU策略，AMV-L在中位/p95延迟上有小幅回退（+26%/+3%），但极端尾部表现更优（p99降低15%，>2s请求减少98%），token开销降低约6%，且检索质量相当（数值差异约0-2%）。性能提升主要源于限制检索集大小和向量搜索工作量，而非缩短提示词。

Conclusion: 长运行LLM代理的可预测性能需要显式控制内存工作集规模并采用价值驱动的生命周期管理，仅依赖保留时间是不够的。AMV-L证明了将内存作为系统资源进行管理可以有效平衡性能与质量。

Abstract: Long-running LLM agents require persistent memory to preserve state across interactions, yet most deployed systems manage memory with age-based retention (e.g., TTL). While TTL bounds item lifetime, it does not bound the computational footprint of memory on the request path: as retained items accumulate, retrieval candidate sets and vector similarity scans can grow unpredictably, yielding heavy-tailed latency and unstable throughput. We present AMV-L (Adaptive Memory Value Lifecycle), a memory-management framework that treats agent memory as a managed systems resource. AMV-L assigns each memory item a continuously updated utility score and uses value-driven promotion, demotion, and eviction to maintain lifecycle tiers; retrieval is restricted to a bounded, tier-aware candidate set that decouples the request-path working set from total retained memory. We implement AMV-L in a full-stack LLM serving system and evaluate it under identical long-running workloads against two baselines: TTL and an LRU working-set policy, with fixed prompt-injection caps. Relative to TTL, AMV-L improves throughput by 3.1x and reduces latency by 4.2x (median), 4.7x (p95), and 4.4x (p99), while reducing the fraction of requests exceeding 2s from 13.8% to 0.007%. Compared to LRU, AMV-L trades a small regression in median/p95 latency (+26% / +3%) for improved extreme-tail behavior (-15% p99; -98% >2s) and lower token overhead (approximately 6% fewer tokens/request), while matching retrieval quality (value means within approximately 0-2%). The gains arise primarily from bounding retrieval-set size and vector-search work, not from shortening prompts. Our results show that predictable performance for long-running LLM agents requires explicit control of memory working-set size and value-driven lifecycle management, rather than retention time alone.

</details>


### [150] [Overcoming Latency-bound Limitations of Distributed Graph Algorithms using the HPX Runtime System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04583)

Result: 基于HPX的实现与GraphX和PBGL进行了对比评估，结果表明：高性能运行时（如HPX）通过利用异步执行、延迟隐藏和共享内存中的细粒度并行性，能够构建显著优于传统框架的算法实现。

We evaluate our HPX-based implementations against GraphX, and PBGL, showing that a high-performance runtime such as HPX enables the construction of algorithms that significantly outperform conventional frameworks by exploiting asynchronous execution, latency hiding, and fine-grained parallelism in shared memory. All algorithms in our prototype follow a unified execution model in which local and remote computations are expressed using the same programming abstractions, with asynchrony managed transparently by the runtime. This design explicitly leverages shared-memory parallelism within each locality while overlapping communication and computation across localities, providing a practical foundation for extending this approach to a broader class of distributed graph algorithms.

### [151] [DuaLip-GPU Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04621)
*Gregory Dexter,Aida Rahmattalabi,Sanjana Garg,Qinquan Song,Ruby Tu,Yuan Gao,Yi Zhang,Zhipeng Wang,Rahul Mazumder*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大规模线性规划求解器（如ECLIPSE和DuaLip）存在架构局限性：与少量模式紧密耦合、基于CPU中心的Scala/Spark技术栈，限制了可扩展性并无法有效利用现代加速器（GPU）。

Method: 1. 设计解耦架构，将问题定义与优化引擎分离，采用算子中心编程模型，通过可组合原语表达LP公式；2. 开发针对稀疏匹配约束的GPU执行技术，包括约束对齐的稀疏布局、批量投影核、仅通信对偶变量的分布式设计；3. 改进脊正则化对偶上升方法，引入Jacobi式行归一化、原始缩放和正则化参数的延拓方案。

Result: 在极端规模匹配工作负载上，GPU实现相比之前的分布式CPU DuaLip求解器在相同停止准则下实现至少10倍的墙钟加速，同时保持收敛保证。

Conclusion: 重新设计的求解器架构成功解决了现有系统的可扩展性和GPU利用率问题，通过解耦设计和GPU优化技术显著提升了大规模线性规划的求解性能，为未来添加新公式提供了灵活的基础架构。

Abstract: Large-scale linear programs (LPs) arise in many decision systems, including ranking, allocation, and matching problems that must be solved repeatedly at massive scale. Prior work such as ECLIPSE and LinkedIn's open-source DuaLip showed that ridge-regularized dual ascent with first-order methods can scale to these settings. However, the original implementation was tightly coupled to a small number of schemas and built on a CPU-centric Scala/Spark stack, limiting extensibility and preventing effective use of modern accelerators.
  We present a redesigned solver architecture that decouples problem specification from the optimization engine and targets GPU execution. The system uses an operator-centric programming model in which LP formulations are expressed through composable primitives for dual objective evaluation and blockwise projection operators for decomposable constraint families. This design allows new formulations to be added locally while reusing a shared optimization loop, diagnostics, and distributed infrastructure.
  To realize the available parallelism, we develop GPU execution techniques tailored to sparse matching constraints, including constraint-aligned sparse layouts, batched projection kernels, and a distributed design that communicates only dual variables. Further, we improve the underlying ridge-regularized dual ascent method with Jacobi-style row normalization, primal scaling, and a continuation scheme for the regularization parameter.
  On extreme-scale matching workloads, the GPU implementation achieves at least a 10x wall-clock speedup over the prior distributed CPU DuaLip solver under matched stopping criteria, while maintaining convergence guarantees.

*Luchang Li,Dongfang Li,Bozhao Gong,Yu Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: P/D架构已成为LLM推理的主流优化策略，但目前缺乏在总吞吐量、服务级别目标(SLO)和请求特征约束下确定最优P/D硬件资源数量的成熟方法论。

Abstract: Prefill-Decode (P/D) disaggregation has emerged as a widely adopted optimization strategy for Large Language Model (LLM) inference. However, there currently exists no well-established methodology for determining the optimal number of P/D hardware resources, subject to constraints on total throughput, service level objectives (SLOs), and request characteristics - specifically input and output lengths. To address this gap, we propose a hybrid approach that combines theoretical modeling with empirical benchmarking. First, we present a theoretical model for calculating P/D resource counts, which is based on total throughput requirements, request input and output lengths, as well as prefill and decode throughput. Then, to obtain the actual prefill and decode throughput under SLO constraints, we model the prefill process using M/M/1 queuing theory, deriving the achieved prefill throughput from the benchmarked maximum prefill throughput and Time-To-First-Token (TTFT). For the decode phase, we determine the decode batch sizes that meet Time-Per-Output-Token (TPOT) requirements and obtain the corresponding decode throughput through empirical measurements. Our experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method can accurately predict optimal P/D resource allocation in real-world LLM inference scenarios.

### [153] [The Semantic Arrow of Time, Part III: RDMA and the Completion Fallacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04774)
*Paul Borrill*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文是《语义时间箭头》系列论文的第三部分，揭示了RDMA技术中存在的"完成谬误"——即RDMA的完成语义保证数据到达远程NIC缓冲区（放置），但不保证数据被接收应用语义集成（提交）。通过分析RDMA写操作的七个时间阶段和四个工业案例（Meta、Google、Microsoft），证明完成信号与应用语义满足之间的差距可任意大，唯有强制反射阶段的协议架构才能消除此差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前两部分论文已识别出计算中隐藏的语义时间箭头和FITO范畴错误，并提出OAE链路状态机作为建设性替代方案。本文旨在研究当这些原则在工业规模上被违反时会发生什么，聚焦于广泛应用于Meta、Google、Microsoft基础设施的高性能数据移动技术RDMA，揭示其完成语义中存在的根本性缺陷。

Method: 通过七个时间阶段分析RDMA Write操作，系统性证明完成信号与应用语义满足之间存在任意大的时间差；采用四个工业案例研究进行实证分析：Meta的RoCE架构、Google的1RMA重设计、Microsoft的DCQCN失败案例、SDR-RDMA部分完成问题；最后对CXL 3.0、NVLink和UALink进行对比分析，评估其对完成谬误的解决程度。

Result: RDMA完成语义包含范畴错误：保证放置但不保证提交，此即"完成谬误"；完成信号与应用语义满足之间的时间差可为任意大；四个工业案例证实该谬误的实际影响；CXL 3.0、NVLink和UALink各自仅部分解决完成谬误，均未完全消除；仅有包含强制反射阶段的协议架构能够弥合交付与提交之间的差距。

Conclusion: RDMA作为工业界最高性能的数据移动技术，其完成语义存在根本性缺陷，即完成谬误。当前主流替代技术（CXL 3.0、NVLink、UALink）均未能彻底解决此问题。要真正消除交付与提交之间的差距，必须采用具有强制反射阶段的协议架构（如前文提出的OAE链路状态机），这为未来高性能互连协议的设计提供了关键指导原则。

Abstract: This is the third of five papers comprising The Semantic Arrow of Time. Parts I and II identified computing's hidden semantic arrow of time, the FITO category mistake, and presented the constructive alternative: the OAE link state machine with its mandatory reflecting phase.
  This paper examines what happens when those principles are violated at industrial scale. Remote Direct Memory Access (RDMA) is the highest-performance data movement technology in production, deployed across Meta's 24,000-GPU clusters, Google's data centers, and Microsoft's Azure infrastructure. We argue that RDMA's completion semantics contain a category mistake: they guarantee placement (data written to a remote NIC buffer) but not commitment (data semantically integrated by the receiving application). We call this the completion fallacy.
  We document the fallacy through seven temporal stages of an RDMA Write operation, showing that the gap between completion signal and application semantic satisfaction can be arbitrarily large. We trace consequences through four case studies: Meta's RoCE fabric, Google's 1RMA redesign, Microsoft's DCQCN failures, and SDR-RDMA partial completions.
  A comparative analysis shows CXL 3.0, NVLink, and UALink each address parts of the completion fallacy but none eliminates it entirely. Only a protocol architecture with a mandatory reflecting phase can close the gap between delivery and commitment.

### [154] [Unlocking Python's Cores: Hardware Usage and Energy Implications of Removing the GIL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04782)
*José Daniel Montoya Salazar*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文研究了禁用Python GIL对能耗和硬件利用率的影响。实验表明：可并行工作负载执行时间最多降低4倍且能耗成比例减少，但内存增加；顺序工作负载能耗增加13-43%；共享对象工作负载因锁竞争收益受限。能耗与执行时间成正比，禁用GIL不显著影响功耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Python 3.13起提供实验性禁用GIL构建，先前研究主要关注性能加速，但对能耗消耗和硬件利用率的影响关注不足。由于多核利用率变化可能影响系统能耗，需全面评估no-GIL构建的实际代价与收益。

Method: 使用Python 3.14.2的GIL和free-threaded两种构建版本，针对四类工作负载（基于NumPy、顺序内核、线程化数值计算、线程化对象操作）测量执行时间、CPU利用率、内存使用和能耗消耗，进行对比分析。

Result: 可并行工作负载：执行时间最多降低4倍，能耗成比例减少，多核利用有效，内存增加。顺序工作负载：无性能收益，能耗增加13-43%。共享对象工作负载：锁竞争导致改进受限或退化。能耗与执行时间成正比。内存使用普遍增加，虚拟内存增加更明显，原因包括每对象锁、线程安全机制和新内存分配器。

Conclusion: Python的no-GIL构建并非普遍改进方案。开发者需评估工作负载是否适合并行执行后再决定是否采用。禁用GIL对可并行任务有显著收益，但对顺序或共享对象密集型任务可能带来能耗惩罚和内存开销。

Abstract: Python's Global Interpreter Lock prevents execution on more than one CPU core at the same time, even when multiple threads are used. However, starting with Python 3.13 an experimental build allows disabling the GIL. While prior work has examined speedup implications of this disabling, the effects on energy consumption and hardware utilization have received less attention. This study measures execution time, CPU utilization, memory usage, and energy consumption using four workload categories: NumPy-based, sequential kernels, threaded numerical workloads, and threaded object workloads, comparing GIL and free-threaded builds of Python 3.14.2.
  The results highlight a trade-off. For parallelizable workloads operating on independent data, the free-threaded build reduces execution time by up to 4 times, with a proportional reduction in energy consumption, and effective multi-core utilization, at the cost of an increase in memory usage. In contrast, sequential workloads do not benefit from removing the GIL and instead show a 13-43% increase in energy consumption. Similarly, workloads where threads frequently access and modify the same objects show reduced improvements or even degradation due to lock contention. Across all workloads, energy consumption is proportional to execution time, indicating that disabling the GIL does not significantly affect power consumption, even when CPU utilization increases. When it comes to memory, the no-GIL build shows a general increase, more visible in virtual memory than in physical memory. This increase is primarily attributed to per-object locking, additional thread-safety mechanisms in the runtime, and the adoption of a new memory allocator.
  These findings suggest that Python's no-GIL build is not a universal improvement. Developers should evaluate whether their workload can effectively benefit from parallel execution before adoption.

</details>

  This paper traces the consequences of the FITO category mistake beyond the data center, into systems people use every day. We examine three domains where forward-only temporal assumptions destroy meaning: file synchronization, where cloud platforms silently delete user content because last-writer-wins cannot represent distributed causality; email, where timestamp-based ordering produces phantom messages, causality violations, and stuck synchronization; and memory--both human and artificial--where reconstructive processes that operate without transactional guarantees produce systematic semantic corruption.
  In each domain, we identify the same structural pattern: a system that commits state changes forward in time without a reflecting phase, and that therefore cannot distinguish between successful semantic integration and mere temporal succession. The pattern is not coincidental. It is the FITO category mistake operating at different scales: bytes in a NIC buffer, files in a cloud, messages in an inbox, engrams in a hippocampus, tokens in a transformer.
  We conclude that the semantic arrow of time is violated whenever a system treats the forward flow of information as sufficient evidence of meaning. Part V will show how the Leibniz Bridge provides a unified framework for closing this gap across all five domains.

Abstract: This is the final paper in the five-part series The Semantic Arrow of Time. Part I identified the FITO category mistake -- treating forward temporal flow as sufficient for establishing meaning. Part II presented the constructive alternative: the OAE link state machine with its mandatory reflecting phase.   We show that this principle dissolves the apparent impossibility of the FLP, Two Generals, and CAP theorems by revealing them as theorems about FITO systems, not about physics. We conclude with open questions and a reflection on what distributed computing looks like when the FITO assumption is dropped.

Motivation: 提示调优已成为提升大语言模型在下游任务性能的重要策略，许多IT企业提供提示调优即服务。然而，现有深度学习资源管理系统无法有效优化大语言模型提示调优工作负载的SLO满足与资源成本降低这两个目标。

Method: 提出PromptTuner系统，包含两个核心创新：(1)设计Prompt Bank以识别高效的初始提示，加速提示调优的收敛过程；(2)开发Workload Scheduler实现快速资源分配，以减少SLO违规和资源成本。

Result: 实验评估表明，与INFless和ElasticFlow相比，PromptTuner分别将SLO违规降低了4.0倍和7.9倍，成本降低了1.6倍和4.5倍。

Conclusion: PromptTuner系统有效解决了大语言模型提示调优场景下的资源管理问题，在满足服务等级目标的同时显著降低了资源供给成本，为提示调优即服务提供了高效的系统解决方案。

Abstract: Prompt tuning has become a prominent strategy for enhancing the performance of Large Language Models (LLMs) on downstream tasks. Many IT enterprises now offer Prompt-Tuning-as-a-Service to fulfill the growing demand for prompt tuning LLMs on downstream tasks. Their primary objective is to satisfy users Service Level Objectives (SLOs) while reducing resource provisioning costs. Nevertheless, our characterization analysis for existing deep learning resource management systems reveals that they are insufficient to optimize these objectives for LLM prompt tuning workloads.
  In this paper, we introduce PromptTuner, an SLO-aware elastic system to optimize LLM prompt tuning. It contains two innovations. (1) We design a Prompt Bank to identify efficient initial prompts to expedite the convergence of prompt tuning. (2) We develop aWorkload Scheduler to enable fast resource allocation to reduce the SLO violation and resource costs. In our evaluation, PromptTuner reduces SLO violations by 4.0x and 7.9x, and lowers costs by 1.6x and 4.5x, compared to INFless and ElasticFlow respectively.

### [158] [Leveraging Structural Knowledge for Solving Election in Anonymous Networks with Shared Randomness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05118)
*Jérémie Chalopin,Emmanuel Godard*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文完全刻画了匿名网络中存在随机化选举算法的条件，涵盖了共享/非共享随机性下的Las Vegas和Monte Carlo算法，并分析了多种结构知识对问题可计算性的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于文献[5]中确定性算法的理论框架进行扩展，针对共享与非共享随机性分别分析Las Vegas和Monte Carlo两类随机算法。考虑共享随机性的推广定义（特定节点子集共享相同随机比特），并针对不同的结构知识类别（如无知识、规模上界、共享源节点数上界、确切规模、完整拓扑等）应用通用刻画。

Result: 获得了随机化选举算法存在的完整充要条件刻画，该结果是文献[8]的完全推广；针对多种具体结构知识类别，推导出相应的算法存在性结论；证明了文献中的随机选举算法均符合本文的理论框架。

Conclusion: 本文提供了匿名网络中随机化选举问题的完整理论图景，清晰揭示了结构知识如何影响问题的可计算性，为共享随机性下的分布式算法设计提供了统一的判定标准。

Abstract: We study the classical Election problem in anonymous net- works, where solutions can rely on the use of random bits, which may be either shared or unshared among nodes. We provide a complete char- acterization of the conditions under which a randomized Election algo- rithm exists, for arbitrary structural knowledge. Our analysis considers both Las Vegas and Monte Carlo randomized algorithms, under the as- sumptions of shared and unshared randomness. In our setting, random sources are considered shared if the output bits are identical across spe- cific subsets of nodes. The algorithms and impossibility proofs are extensions of those of [5] for the deterministic setting. Our results are a complete generalization of those from [8]. Moreover, as applications, we consider many specific knowledge: no knowledge, a bound on the size, a bound on the number of nodes sharing a source, the size, or the full topology of the network. For each of them, we show how the general characterizations apply, showing they actually correspond to classes of structural knowledge. We also de- scribe also how randomized Election algorithms from the literature fits in this landscape. We therefore provide a comprehensive picture illustrating how knowledge influences the computability of the Election problem in arbitrary anonymous graphs with shared randomness.

### [161] [Radiation Hydrodynamics at Scale: Comparing MPI and Asynchronous Many-Task Runtimes with FleCSI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05366)
*Alexander Strack,Hartmut Kaiser,Dirk Pflüger*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文对FleCSI框架的三种并行后端（MPI、Legion、HPX）进行了大规模基准测试评估。结果表明，MPI后端在通信密集型应用中效率最高（97%并行效率），HPX后端在计算密集型应用中表现优异（最高1.64倍加速），而Legion后端存在显著开销和扩展性限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编写高效的分布式代码仍然是一项劳动密集型且复杂的工作。为简化应用开发，FleCSI框架提供了基于任务运行时模型的高级编程接口，集成了MPI、Legion和HPX等先进并行化后端。本研究旨在量化异步多任务运行时（AMTR）后端带来的优势和开销，为用户选择合适的后端提供依据。

Method: 在最多1024个节点上，使用FleCSI框架的三种后端（MPI、Legion、HPX）对两个代表性应用进行基准测试：一个是通信密集型的简单泊松求解器，另一个是计算密集型的多维辐射流体动力学代码HARD。通过弱扩展性和强扩展性测试，比较各后端的性能、开销和扩展能力。

Result: 在泊松求解器测试中，MPI后端在131072核心上实现超过97%的弱扩展并行效率，表明抽象层开销极小。Legion后端存在显著开销和扩展限制。HPX后端相比MPI+Kokkos仅有边际开销，但受限于非优化的HPX集合操作。在辐射流体动力学测试中，HPX后端在少于64节点时性能超越MPI+Kokkos，弱扩展平均加速1.31倍，强扩展最高加速1.27倍；在纯流体动力学测试中，HPX在少于32节点时相比MPI加速1.20倍，相比MPI+Kokkos加速高达1.64倍。

Conclusion: FleCSI框架的抽象层开销极低，适合高性能计算应用。不同后端各有优势：MPI后端适合通信密集型任务且扩展性最佳；HPX后端在计算密集型任务和小规模集群上表现优异，但需要优化集合操作以提升扩展性；Legion后端目前存在性能瓶颈。用户应根据应用特点（通信密集或计算密集）和规模选择合适的后端。

Abstract: Writing efficient distributed code remains a labor-intensive and complex endeavor. To simplify application development, the Flexible Computational Science Infrastructure (FleCSI) framework offers a user-oriented, high-level programming interface that is built upon a task-based runtime model. Internally, FleCSI integrates state-of-the-art parallelization backends, including MPI and the asynchronous many-task runtimes (AMTRs) Legion and HPX, enabling applications to fully leverage asynchronous parallelism. In this work, we benchmark two applications using FleCSI's three backends on up to 1024 nodes, intending to quantify the advantages and overheads introduced by the AMTR backends. As representative applications, we select a simple Poisson solver and the multidimensional radiation hydrodynamics code HARD. In the communication-focused Poisson solver benchmark, FleCSI achieves over 97% parallel efficiency using the MPI backend under weak scaling on up to 131072 cores, indicating that only minimal overhead is introduced by its abstraction layer. While the Legion backend exhibits notable overheads and scaling limitations, the HPX backend introduces only marginal overhead compared to MPI+Kokkos. However, the scalability of the HPX backend is currently limited due to the usage of non-optimized HPX collective operations. In the computation-focused radiation hydrodynamics benchmarks, the performance gap between the MPI and HPX backends fades. On fewer than 64 nodes, the HPX backend outperforms MPI+Kokkos, achieving an average speedup of 1.31 under weak scaling and up to 1.27 under strong scaling. For the hydrodynamics-only HARD benchmark, the HPX backend demonstrates superior performance on fewer than 32 nodes, achieving speedups of up to 1.20 relative to MPI and up to 1.64 relative to MPI+Kokkos.

### [162] [Decorrelating the Future: Joint Frequency Domain Learning for Spatio-temporal Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04418)
*Zepu Wang,Bowen Liao,Jeff,Ban*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了FreST Loss，一种基于联合傅里叶变换的频域增强时空训练目标，通过在联合时空谱域中对齐预测与真值，有效解耦复杂的时空依赖关系，在六个真实数据集上持续提升SOTA基线性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准直接预测模型通常依赖点对点目标（如MSE），无法捕获图结构信号中固有的复杂时空依赖性；现有频域方法（如FreDF）虽缓解了时间自相关问题，但往往忽略空间和跨时空交互。

Method: 提出FreST Loss，一种频域增强的时空训练目标，利用联合傅里叶变换（JFT）将监督扩展到联合时空谱域，在统一频谱域中对齐模型预测与真值，有效解耦空间和时间上的复杂依赖关系。

Result: 理论分析表明该公式能减少时域训练目标相关的估计偏差；在六个真实世界数据集上的大量实验表明，FreST Loss具有模型无关性，能够持续提升最先进基线模型的性能。

Conclusion: FreST Loss通过在联合时空谱域进行监督，有效解决了传统时域目标函数忽略复杂时空依赖的问题，为图结构信号的预测任务提供了一种通用且有效的训练目标改进方案。

Abstract: Standard direct forecasting models typically rely on point-wise objectives such as Mean Squared Error, which fail to capture the complex spatio-temporal dependencies inherent in graph-structured signals. While recent frequency-domain approaches such as FreDF mitigate temporal autocorrelation, they often overlook spatial and cross spatio-temporal interactions. To address this limitation, we propose FreST Loss, a frequency-enhanced spatio-temporal training objective that extends supervision to the joint spatio-temporal spectrum. By leveraging the Joint Fourier Transform (JFT), FreST Loss aligns model predictions with ground truth in a unified spectral domain, effectively decorrelating complex dependencies across both space and time. Theoretical analysis shows that this formulation reduces estimation bias associated with time-domain training objectives. Extensive experiments on six real-world datasets demonstrate that FreST Loss is model-agnostic and consistently improves state-of-the-art baselines by better capturing holistic spatio-temporal dynamics.

</details>


### [163] [Machine Learning for Complex Systems Dynamics: Detecting Bifurcations in Dynamical Systems with Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04420)
*Swadesh Pal,Roderick Melnik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于深度神经网络的平衡信息神经网络(EINNs)方法，通过逆向映射从平衡状态推断系统参数，从而高效检测复杂动力系统中的临界转换和突变点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的临界转换检测方法（如前向模拟或分岔分析）计算成本高、参数采样受限，亟需一种高效、灵活的替代方法来识别系统发生灾难性转变的临界阈值。

Method: 提出平衡信息神经网络(EINNs)，该方法逆向传统思路——以候选平衡状态作为输入，训练深度神经网络推断满足平衡条件的对应系统参数。通过分析学习到的参数景观并观察平衡映射在可行性或连续性上的突变，有效检测临界阈值。

Result: 在具有鞍结分岔和多稳定性的非线性系统上进行验证，证明EINNs能够准确恢复与即将发生转变相关的参数区域，有效识别临界阈值。

Conclusion: EINNs方法为高维和非线性系统中临界转换的早期检测与结构分析提供了一种灵活的替代方案，相比传统技术具有明显优势。

Abstract: Critical transitions are the abrupt shifts between qualitatively different states of a system, and they are crucial to understanding tipping points in complex dynamical systems across ecology, climate science, and biology. Detecting these shifts typically involves extensive forward simulations or bifurcation analyses, which are often computationally intensive and limited by parameter sampling. In this study, we propose a novel machine learning approach based on deep neural networks (DNNs) called equilibrium-informed neural networks (EINNs) to identify critical thresholds associated with catastrophic regime shifts. Rather than fixing parameters and searching for solutions, the EINN method reverses this process by using candidate equilibrium states as inputs and training a DNN to infer the corresponding system parameters that satisfy the equilibrium condition. By analyzing the learned parameter landscape and observing abrupt changes in the feasibility or continuity of equilibrium mappings, critical thresholds can be effectively detected. We demonstrate this capability on nonlinear systems exhibiting saddle-node bifurcations and multi-stability, showing that EINNs can recover the parameter regions associated with impending transitions. This method provides a flexible alternative to traditional techniques, offering new insights into the early detection and structure of critical shifts in high-dimensional and nonlinear systems.

</details>


### [164] [FedEMA-Distill: Exponential Moving Average Guided Knowledge Distillation for Robust Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04422)
*Hamza Reguieg,Mohamed El Kamili,Essaid Sabir*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出FedEMA-Distill，一种服务端联邦学习框架，通过结合全局模型的指数移动平均（EMA）和基于公共代理数据集的集成知识蒸馏，有效解决了非独立同分布（non-IID）数据和恶意客户端带来的性能下降问题，在提升准确率的同时显著降低通信开销并增强抗攻击能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习在实际部署中面临三大核心挑战：（1）客户端数据异构性（non-IID）导致客户端漂移和收敛缓慢；（2）恶意客户端的存在威胁系统鲁棒性；（3）高昂的通信开销。现有方法往往难以同时解决这些问题，且通常需要修改客户端软件或限制模型架构一致性。

Method: 提出FedEMA-Distill服务端框架，包含三个关键组件：（1）服务端维护全局模型的指数移动平均（EMA）以实现时序平滑；（2）客户端仅上传在公共代理数据集上的压缩预测logits，支持异构模型架构且无需修改客户端训练流程；（3）服务端采用坐标中位数或修剪均值聚合logits以抵御Byzantine攻击，并通过集成知识蒸馏更新全局模型。该设计兼容安全聚合和差分隐私。

Result: 在CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100、FEMNIST和AG News数据集上的Dirichlet-0.1标签偏斜实验表明：（1）Top-1准确率提升显著（CIFAR-10最高+5%，CIFAR-100最高+6%）；（2）达到目标准确率所需通信轮次减少30-35%；（3）每轮客户端上行负载降至0.09-0.46 MB，比传输完整模型权重低约一个数量级；（4）在10-20% Byzantine客户端攻击下保持稳定训练和良好校准的预测。

Conclusion: FedEMA-Distill通过时序平滑与仅logits聚合的协同作用，构建了一个通信高效、抗攻击鲁棒且部署友好的联邦学习流程。该方法无需修改客户端软件、支持模型异构性，并与安全聚合和差分隐私兼容，为实际联邦学习部署提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) often degrades when clients hold heterogeneous non-Independent and Identically Distributed (non-IID) data and when some clients behave adversarially, leading to client drift, slow convergence, and high communication overhead. This paper proposes FedEMA-Distill, a server-side procedure that combines an exponential moving average (EMA) of the global model with ensemble knowledge distillation from client-uploaded prediction logits evaluated on a small public proxy dataset. Clients run standard local training, upload only compressed logits, and may use different model architectures, so no changes are required to client-side software while still supporting model heterogeneity across devices. Experiments on CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, FEMNIST, and AG News under Dirichlet-0.1 label skew show that FedEMA-Distill improves top-1 accuracy by several percentage points (up to +5% on CIFAR-10 and +6% on CIFAR-100) over representative baselines, reaches a given target accuracy in 30-35% fewer communication rounds, and reduces per-round client uplink payloads to 0.09-0.46 MB, i.e., roughly an order of magnitude less than transmitting full model weights. Using coordinate-wise median or trimmed-mean aggregation of logits at the server further stabilizes training in the presence of up to 10-20% Byzantine clients and yields well-calibrated predictions under attack. These results indicate that coupling temporal smoothing with logits-only aggregation provides a communication-efficient and attack-resilient FL pipeline that is deployment-friendly and compatible with secure aggregation and differential privacy, since only aggregated or obfuscated model outputs are exchanged.

</details>


### [165] [Delta-Crosscoder: Robust Crosscoder Model Diffing in Narrow Fine-Tuning Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04426)
*Aly Kassem,Thomas Jiralerspong,Negar Rostamzadeh,Golnoosh Farnadi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Delta-Crosscoder方法，通过结合BatchTopK稀疏性和基于delta的损失函数，有效识别并隔离导致微调后行为变化的潜在方向，在10个模型实验中表现优于SAE基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型差异识别方法（Crosscoders）在处理狭窄微调（narrow fine-tuning）场景时存在困难，此时行为变化具有局部性和不对称性，现有方法难以准确捕捉这种变化。

Method: 提出Delta-Crosscoder方法，该方法结合了三个关键组件：(1) BatchTopK稀疏性约束；(2) 基于delta的损失函数，优先关注模型间变化的方向；(3) 利用匹配输入上的成对激活产生的隐式对比信号。

Result: 在10个模型有机体上评估（包括合成虚假事实、涌现性不对齐、阈下学习、禁忌词猜测等任务；涵盖Gemma、LLaMA、Qwen模型，参数量1B-9B），Delta-Crosscoder能够可靠地分离出导致微调行为的因果性潜在方向，并实现有效缓解，性能优于SAE基线方法，与非SAE方法相当。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，Crosscoders仍然是模型差异识别的强大工具，Delta-Crosscoder有效解决了狭窄微调场景下的挑战，为理解微调如何改变模型内部表示提供了有效方法。

Abstract: Model diffing methods aim to identify how fine-tuning changes a model's internal representations. Crosscoders approach this by learning shared dictionaries of interpretable latent directions between base and fine-tuned models. However, existing formulations struggle with narrow fine-tuning, where behavioral changes are localized and asymmetric. We introduce Delta-Crosscoder, which combines BatchTopK sparsity with a delta-based loss prioritizing directions that change between models, plus an implicit contrastive signal from paired activations on matched inputs. Evaluated across 10 model organisms, including synthetic false facts, emergent misalignment, subliminal learning, and taboo word guessing (Gemma, LLaMA, Qwen; 1B-9B parameters), Delta-Crosscoder reliably isolates latent directions causally responsible for fine-tuned behaviors and enables effective mitigation, outperforming SAE-based baselines, while matching the Non-SAE-based. Our results demonstrate that crosscoders remain a powerful tool for model diffing.

### [166] [Thin Keys, Full Values: Reducing KV Cache via Low-Dimensional Attention Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04427)
*Hengshuai Yao,Guan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出非对称注意力机制，将查询/键的选择维度与值的语义传递维度解耦，通过理论和实验证明选择操作仅需低维表示。在多个模型和任务上验证，可实现75%的KV缓存节省，仅损失不到2%的质量，显著提升服务并发能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Transformer注意力机制强制查询、键、值使用相同维度（d_q = d_k = d_v），但作者指出这三者功能本质不同：查询和键负责生成注意力权重（选择操作），而值负责传递丰富的语义表示。选择操作本质上是低维操作，维持维度对称性是不必要的，这为模型压缩和效率提升提供了理论依据。

Method: 提出非对称注意力设计：选择维度（d_select）可远小于模型维度。理论论证选择N个相关模式仅需O(log N)维度。通过七组实验验证：位置选择任务、内容检索、WikiText语言建模、GPT-2后训练SVD压缩、LLaMA-125M验证、Mistral-7B大规模验证。对已有模型采用SVD压缩键矩阵，配合少量数据（3轮训练）的QK微调恢复性能。

Result: 实验表明：位置选择每头仅需1维，内容检索约需log₂N维；语言建模中d_select = d_model/4仅导致4.3%困惑度增加并减少75%的QK参数；键比查询更易压缩；在Mistral-7B（7.2B参数）上实现75%键缓存节省，残余质量损失仅2.0%；对于128K上下文的7B模型，每个用户节省25GB KV缓存，支持约60%更多并发用户。

Conclusion: 查询/键的选择功能可大幅降维而不显著影响性能，这挑战了Transformer维度对称性的传统假设。非对称注意力为KV缓存优化提供有效方案，通过SVD压缩+QK微调的实用流程，在不重新训练模型的前提下实现显著的内存节省和吞吐量提升，具有重要实际应用价值。

Abstract: Standard transformer attention uses identical dimensionality for queries, keys, and values ($d_q = d_k = d_v = \dmodel$). Our insight is that these components serve fundamentally different roles, and this symmetry is unnecessary. Queries and keys produce scalar attention weights (\emph{selection}), while values carry rich semantic representations (\emph{value transfer}). We argue that selection is an inherently lower-dimensional operation than value transfer, requiring only $\BigO(\log N)$ dimensions to distinguish among $N$ relevant patterns. We validate this hypothesis across seven experiments: (1)~positional selection tasks requiring just 1~dimension per head, (2)~content-based retrieval requiring $\sim\!\log_2 N$ dimensions, (3--4)~WikiText-2 and WikiText-103 language modeling where $\dselect = \dmodel/4$ incurs only 4.3\% perplexity increase while reducing QK parameters by 75\%, (5)~post-training SVD compression of GPT-2, revealing keys to be far more compressible than queries, with lightweight QK fine-tuning recovering nearly all quality loss, (6)~a 125M-parameter LLaMA model confirming identical degradation ratios across architectures, and (7)~Mistral-7B (7.2B parameters), where SVD compression followed by QK fine-tuning achieves 75\% key cache savings at just 2.0\% residual quality cost. For existing models, SVD compression followed by QK fine-tuning (3 epochs on a small fraction of pretraining data) achieves 75\% key cache savings at $<$2\% residual quality cost. For a 7B-parameter model serving 128K context, asymmetric attention saves 25\,GB of KV cache per user, enabling approximately 60\% more concurrent users on the same GPU.

</details>


### [167] [MCEL: Margin-Based Cross-Entropy Loss for Error-Tolerant Quantized Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05048)
*Mikail Yayla,Akash Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型损失函数MCEL（Margin Cross-Entropy Loss），通过在logit层面显式促进分类间隔（margin）分离来提升神经网络对位错误的容错能力。该方法无需在训练时注入错误，实现简单高效，可作为标准交叉熵损失的直接替代，在1%错误率下准确率提升高达15%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通过训练时注入位翻转来提升神经网络容错能力的方法存在计算开销大、高错误率下精度下降明显、对大型网络扩展性差等问题，难以满足未来近似计算平台和易错存储技术的需求。因此需要探索无需错误感知训练的容错机制。

Method: 本文首先建立了位错误容错能力与输出层分类间隔之间的直接联系。基于此洞察，提出了间隔交叉熵损失（MCEL），该损失函数在保留标准交叉熵损失良好优化特性的同时，显式促进logit层面的间隔分离。MCEL引入了一个可解释的间隔参数，可以以有原则的方式调节鲁棒性。该方法可作为标准交叉熵损失的即插即用替代品。

Result: 在多个不同复杂度的数据集、多种神经网络架构和不同量化方案上进行了广泛实验评估。结果表明MCEL显著提升了位错误容错能力，在1%的错误率下准确率提升高达15%。方法实现简单、高效，具有良好扩展性。

Conclusion: MCEL为训练时位翻转注入提供了一种可扩展且有原则的替代方案，不仅实现了更好的容错性能，还深入揭示了神经网络鲁棒性的来源，为在近似计算和存储系统上更高效地部署神经网络提供了新思路。

Abstract: Robustness to bit errors is a key requirement for the reliable use of neural networks (NNs) on emerging approximate computing platforms and error-prone memory technologies. A common approach to achieve bit error tolerance in NNs is injecting bit flips during training according to a predefined error model. While effective in certain scenarios, training-time bit flip injection introduces substantial computational overhead, often degrades inference accuracy at high error rates, and scales poorly for larger NN architectures. These limitations make error injection an increasingly impractical solution for ensuring robustness on future approximate computing platforms and error-prone memory technologies. In this work, we investigate the mechanisms that enable NNs to tolerate bit errors without relying on error-aware training. We establish a direct connection between bit error tolerance and classification margins at the output layer. Building on this insight, we propose a novel loss function, the Margin Cross-Entropy Loss (MCEL), which explicitly promotes logit-level margin separation while preserving the favorable optimization properties of the standard cross-entropy loss. Furthermore, MCEL introduces an interpretable margin parameter that allows robustness to be tuned in a principled manner. Extensive experimental evaluations across multiple datasets of varying complexity, diverse NN architectures, and a range of quantization schemes demonstrate that MCEL substantially improves bit error tolerance, up to 15 % in accuracy for an error rate of 1 %. Our proposed MCEL method is simple to implement, efficient, and can be integrated as a drop-in replacement for standard CEL. It provides a scalable and principled alternative to training-time bit flip injection, offering new insights into the origins of NN robustness and enabling more efficient deployment on approximate computing and memory systems.

</details>


### [168] [Agent Memory Below the Prompt: Persistent Q4 KV Cache for Multi-Agent LLM Inference on Edge Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04428)
*Yakov Pyotr Shkolnikov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对边缘设备上多智能体LLM系统的内存瓶颈问题，提出了一种将KV缓存持久化到磁盘并使用4-bit量化格式存储的方案，通过直接恢复缓存避免冗余预填充计算，将首令牌时间(TTFT)降低高达136倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘设备RAM不足以同时容纳所有智能体的KV缓存。在Apple M4 Pro上，10.2GB缓存预算仅能容纳3个智能体(8K上下文，FP16)。10智能体工作流需要频繁驱逐和重载缓存，每次驱逐导致完整重新预填充，在4K上下文时每个智能体需15.7秒。

Method: 系统包含三个核心组件：(1) 块池(Block Pool)：以safetensors格式提供每个智能体隔离的Q4 KV缓存；(2) BatchQuantizedKVCache：支持多智能体量化缓存的并发推理；(3) 跨阶段上下文注入：在对话阶段间累积注意力状态而无需重新计算。通过将KV缓存以4-bit量化格式持久化到磁盘并直接加载到注意力层，消除冗余O(n)预填充计算。

Result: 在三种架构上评估(Gemma 3 12B、DeepSeek-Coder-V2-Lite 16B、Llama 3.1 8B)：缓存恢复将首令牌时间降低高达136倍(Gemma: 22-136倍@4K-32K; DeepSeek: 11-76倍@4K-32K; Llama: 24-111倍@4K-16K; 3-10倍@1K)。Q4量化在固定内存中容纳的智能体上下文数量是FP16的4倍。实际Q4 KV缓存的困惑度影响：Gemma -0.7%，Llama +2.8%，DeepSeek +3.0%。

Conclusion: 通过KV缓存持久化和4-bit量化，成功解决了边缘设备多智能体LLM系统的内存管理问题，显著降低了延迟并提升了内存效率，同时保持了可接受的模型质量。代码已开源。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems on edge devices face a memory management problem: device RAM is too small to hold every agent's KV cache simultaneously. On Apple M4 Pro with 10.2 GB of cache budget, only 3 agents fit at 8K context in FP16. A 10-agent workflow must constantly evict and reload caches. Without persistence, every eviction forces a full re-prefill through the model -- 15.7 seconds per agent at 4K context. We address this by persisting each agent's KV cache to disk in 4-bit quantized format and reloading it directly into the attention layer, eliminating redundant O(n) prefill computation via direct cache restoration. The system comprises three components: a block pool providing per-agent isolated Q4 KV caches in safetensors format, a BatchQuantizedKVCache for concurrent inference over multiple agents' quantized caches, and cross-phase context injection that accumulates attention state across conversation phases without re-computation. Evaluated on three architectures (Gemma 3 12B, dense GQA, 48 layers; DeepSeek-Coder-V2-Lite 16B, MoE MLA, 27 layers; Llama 3.1 8B, dense GQA, 32 layers), cache restoration reduces time-to-first-token by up to 136x (Gemma: 22--136x at 4K--32K; DeepSeek: 11--76x at 4K--32K; Llama: 24--111x at 4K--16K; 3--10x at 1K). Q4 quantization fits 4x more agent contexts into fixed device memory than FP16. Perplexity measured with actual Q4 KV caches shows -0.7% for Gemma, +2.8% for Llama, and +3.0% for DeepSeek. Open-source at https://github.com/yshk-mxim/agent-memory

</details>


### [169] [Flowers: A Warp Drive for Neural PDE Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04430)
*Till Muser,Alexandra Spitzer,Matti Lassas,Maarten V. de Hoop,Ivan Dokmanić*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了Flowers，一种完全基于多头变形（multihead warps）的神经网络架构，用于学习偏微分方程（PDE）解算子。该架构不依赖傅里叶乘数、点积注意力或卷积混合，仅通过点wise位移场预测和稀疏采样实现全局交互，具有线性计算成本。实验表明，1700万参数的模型在2D和3D时间依赖PDE基准测试中表现优异，1.5亿参数版本超越了更大的基于Transformer的基础模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PDE求解神经网络架构（如傅里叶神经算子、卷积网络、Transformer）存在计算成本高或局部性限制的问题。本文受物理启发，旨在设计一种既能实现自适应全局交互，又能保持线性计算成本的架构，通过变形机制在空间中高效传递信息，同时保持物理守恒律的特性。

Method: Flowers架构的核心是多头部变形机制：每个头部预测一个位移场并对混合输入特征进行变形操作。位移场通过点wise方式预测（无空间聚合），非局部性仅通过每个头部在源坐标处的单次稀疏采样引入。架构采用点wise通道混合和多尺度支架结构，通过在多尺度残差块中堆叠变形层实现全局自适应交互。设计从三个角度获得理论支撑：守恒律的流映射、非均匀介质中的波动方程、以及动力学理论的连续极限。

Result: Flowers在广泛的2D和3D时间依赖PDE基准测试中取得优异性能，尤其在流体流动和波动问题中表现突出。紧凑的1700万参数模型一致性地超越了相似规模的傅里叶、卷积和基于注意力的基线模型。1.5亿参数版本在性能上超越了参数量更大、训练数据和计算资源更多的最新基于Transformer的基础模型。

Conclusion: Flowers证明了完全基于变形机制的神经架构可以高效且有效地学习PDE解算子。该架构通过点wise位移预测和稀疏采样实现了线性成本的全局交互，为PDE求解提供了一个物理启发、计算高效的替代方案，在保持模型紧凑性的同时达到了最先进性能。

Abstract: We introduce Flowers, a neural architecture for learning PDE solution operators built entirely from multihead warps. Aside from pointwise channel mixing and a multiscale scaffold, Flowers use no Fourier multipliers, no dot-product attention, and no convolutional mixing. Each head predicts a displacement field and warps the mixed input features. Motivated by physics and computational efficiency, displacements are predicted pointwise, without any spatial aggregation, and nonlocality enters \emph{only} through sparse sampling at source coordinates, \emph{one} per head. Stacking warps in multiscale residual blocks yields Flowers, which implement adaptive, global interactions at linear cost. We theoretically motivate this design through three complementary lenses: flow maps for conservation laws, waves in inhomogeneous media, and a kinetic-theoretic continuum limit. Flowers achieve excellent performance on a broad suite of 2D and 3D time-dependent PDE benchmarks, particularly flows and waves. A compact 17M-parameter model consistently outperforms Fourier, convolution, and attention-based baselines of similar size, while a 150M-parameter variant improves over recent transformer-based foundation models with much more parameters, data, and training compute.

### [170] [Uncertainty-Calibrated Spatiotemporal Field Diffusion with Sparse Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04431)
*Kevin Valencia,Xihaier Luo,Shinjae Yoo,David Keetae Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了SOLID，一个基于掩码条件的扩散模型框架，专门用于处理仅有稀疏观测数据时的时空场预测和重建问题，无需密集场数据即可端到端训练，在极端稀疏条件下实现了显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理场的观测数据通常仅来自稀疏且时变的传感器位置，导致预测和重建问题具有不适定性和高度不确定性。现有方法依赖密集的再分析数据或模拟数据进行训练，仅在测试时处理稀疏性，这与实际应用场景不符。

Method: 提出了SOLID框架：1) 掩码条件扩散模型，每个去噪步骤以测量值及其位置为条件；2) 双掩码目标函数，强调在未观测区域的学习，同时对输入和目标重叠的可靠锚点区域加权；3) 严格的稀疏条件路径实现后验采样；4) 仅使用稀疏监督进行端到端训练，无需密集场或预填充。

Result: 在极端稀疏条件下：1) 概率误差降低一个数量级；2) 生成校准良好的不确定性图（可靠性指数\r{ho} > 0.7）；3) 成功采样出与观测值一致的全场分布。

Conclusion: SOLID证明了仅利用稀疏观测数据训练时空动力学模型的可行性，为实际物理场监测和预测提供了更符合现实约束的解决方案，在不确定性量化方面展现出优异性能。

Abstract: Physical fields are typically observed only at sparse, time-varying sensor locations, making forecasting and reconstruction ill-posed and uncertainty-critical. We present SOLID, a mask-conditioned diffusion framework that learns spatiotemporal dynamics from sparse observations alone: training and evaluation use only observed target locations, requiring no dense fields and no pre-imputation. Unlike prior work that trains on dense reanalysis or simulations and only tests under sparsity, SOLID is trained end-to-end with sparse supervision only. SOLID conditions each denoising step on the measured values and their locations, and introduces a dual-masking objective that (i) emphasizes learning in unobserved void regions while (ii) upweights overlap pixels where inputs and targets provide the most reliable anchors. This strict sparse-conditioning pathway enables posterior sampling of full fields consistent with the measurements, achieving up to an order-of-magnitude improvement in probabilistic error and yielding calibrated uncertainty maps (\r{ho} > 0.7) under severe sparsity.

### [171] [Competitive Multi-Operator Reinforcement Learning for Joint Pricing and Fleet Rebalancing in AMoD Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05000)

Method: 提出多运营商强化学习框架，使两个运营商同时学习定价和车队再平衡策略；整合离散选择理论，通过效用最大化决策实现乘客分配和需求竞争的内生涌现。

Abstract: Autonomous Mobility-on-Demand (AMoD) systems promise to revolutionize urban transportation by providing affordable on-demand services to meet growing travel demand. However, realistic AMoD markets will be competitive, with multiple operators competing for passengers through strategic pricing and fleet deployment. While reinforcement learning has shown promise in optimizing single-operator AMoD control, existing work fails to capture competitive market dynamics. We investigate the impact of competition on policy learning by introducing a multi-operator reinforcement learning framework where two operators simultaneously learn pricing and fleet rebalancing policies. By integrating discrete choice theory, we enable passenger allocation and demand competition to emerge endogenously from utility-maximizing decisions. Experiments using real-world data from multiple cities demonstrate that competition fundamentally alters learned behaviors, leading to lower prices and distinct fleet positioning patterns compared to monopolistic settings. Notably, we demonstrate that learning-based approaches are robust to the additional stochasticity of competition, with competitive agents successfully converging to effective policies while accounting for partially unobserved competitor strategies.

</details>


### [172] [ZorBA: Zeroth-order Federated Fine-tuning of LLMs with Heterogeneous Block Activation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04436)
*Chuiyang Meng,Ming Tang,Vincent W. S. Wong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了ZorBA框架，通过零阶优化和异构模块激活机制，解决了联邦微调大语言模型中的显存占用高和通信开销大问题，在显存使用上降低了最多62.41%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的联邦微调面临两大挑战：一是由于模型参数量巨大，本地更新会产生极高的显存(VRAM)消耗；二是频繁的模型交换会导致显著的通信开销。

Method: 提出了ZorBA框架，包含三个核心设计：(1)利用零阶优化通过前向传播消除客户端梯度存储需求；(2)设计异构模块激活机制，由中央服务器向不同客户端分配不同的Transformer模块子集，以加速收敛并降低显存占用；(3)利用共享随机种子和梯度有限差分技术减少通信开销。同时建立了理论分析框架，形式化优化问题以优化模块激活决策，并提出ε-约束字典序算法求解。

Result: 实验结果表明，ZorBA在显存使用上比三个联邦微调基线方法最多降低62.41%，同时保持了较低的通信开销。理论分析刻画了模块激活决策对收敛速度和显存使用的影响。

Conclusion: ZorBA有效解决了联邦大语言模型微调中的显存和通信瓶颈问题，为零阶优化与异构模块激活的协同设计提供了理论指导和实践验证，为资源受限场景下的联邦微调提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Federated fine-tuning of large language models (LLMs) enables collaborative tuning across distributed clients. However, due to the large size of LLMs, local updates in federated learning (FL) may incur substantial video random-access memory (VRAM) usage. Moreover, frequent model exchange may lead to significant communication overhead. To tackle these challenges, in this paper we propose ZorBA, a zeroth-order optimization-based federated fine-tuning framework with heterogeneous block activation. ZorBA leverages zeroth-order optimization to eliminate the storage of gradients at the clients by forward passes. ZorBA includes a heterogeneous block activation mechanism in which the central server allocates different subsets of transformer blocks to clients in order to accelerate the convergence rate and reduce the VRAM usage. Furthermore, ZorBA utilizes shared random seeds and the finite differences of gradients in order to reduce the communication overhead. We conduct theoretical analysis to characterize the effect of block activation decisions on the convergence rate and VRAM usage. To jointly enhance the convergence rate and reduce the VRAM usage, we formulate an optimization problem to optimize the block activation decisions. We propose an $ε$-constraint lexicographic algorithm to solve this problem. Experimental results show that ZorBA outperforms three federated fine-tuning baselines in VRAM usage by up to 62.41% and incurs a low communication overhead.

However, the limited computation resources of the clients may result in a high delay and energy consumption on training. ASFL exploits the computation resources of the central server to train part of the model and enables adaptive model splitting as well as resource allocation during training. To optimize the learning performance (i.e., convergence rate) and efficiency (i.e., delay and energy consumption) of ASFL, we theoretically analyze the convergence rate and formulate a joint learning performance and resource allocation optimization problem. Solving this problem is challenging due to the long-term delay and energy consumption constraints as well as the coupling of the model splitting and resource allocation decisions. We propose an online optimization enhanced block coordinate descent (OOE-BCD) algorithm to solve the problem iteratively. Experimental results show that when compared with five baseline schemes, our proposed ASFL framework converges faster and reduces the total delay and energy consumption by up to 75% and 80%, respectively.

### [175] [On Emergences of Non-Classical Statistical Characteristics in Classical Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04451)
*Hanyu Zhao,Yang Wu,Yuexian Hou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 受量子力学中测量不相容性和Bell不等式启发，本文提出了非经典网络（NCnet），发现共享隐藏层的多任务梯度竞争会产生非经典统计行为（CHSH不等式S值>2），揭示了任务间通过损失振荡形成的隐式非局域关联，并指出S值可作为模型容量与泛化性能的指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受量子力学中测量不相容性（measurement incompatibility）和Bell族不等式的启发，作者希望探索经典神经网络是否能展现类似的非经典统计行为，并利用这一视角理解深度网络的内部交互与训练动力学。

Method: 提出非经典网络（NCnet），一种简单的经典神经架构；在可解释的实验设置下，通过CHSH不等式的S统计量量化非经典性；分析多任务共享隐藏层神经元的梯度竞争机制，以及任务头之间通过局部损失振荡实现的隐式感知。

Result: （1）非经典性源于多任务共享隐藏层神经元的梯度竞争；（2）即使无物理通信链路，任务头可通过局部损失振荡隐式感知其他任务，形成训练结果的非局域关联；（3）S值随资源变化呈现三阶段：低资源时逐步增至经典上界2，临界尺度附近可暂时超过2，高资源时渐近衰减至2附近波动；（4）模型容量不足时，S值与泛化性能正相关，S首次接近2的区间往往对应良好泛化。

Conclusion: 非经典统计行为可由经典神经网络产生，为理解深度网络的内部交互与训练动力学提供了新视角；S值可作为泛化性能的潜在指标，临界资源区域附近的非经典性与模型性能密切相关。

Abstract: Inspired by measurement incompatibility and Bell-family inequalities in quantum mechanics, we propose the Non-Classical Network (NCnet), a simple classical neural architecture that stably exhibits non-classical statistical behaviors under typical and interpretable experimental setups. We find non-classicality, measured by the $S$ statistic of CHSH inequality, arises from gradient competitions of hidden-layer neurons shared by multi-tasks. Remarkably, even without physical links supporting explicit communication, one task head can implicitly sense the training task of other task heads via local loss oscillations, leading to non-local correlations in their training outcomes. Specifically, in the low-resource regime, the value of $S$ increases gradually with increasing resources and approaches toward its classical upper-bound 2, which implies that underfitting is alleviated with resources increase. As the model nears the critical scale required for adequate performance, $S$ may temporarily exceed 2. As resources continue to grow, $S$ then asymptotically decays down to and fluctuates around 2. Empirically, when model capacity is insufficient, $S$ is positively correlated with generalization performance, and the regime where $S$ first approaches $2$ often corresponding to good generalization. Overall, our results suggest that non-classical statistics can provide a novel perspective for understanding internal interactions and training dynamics of deep networks.

### [176] [Learning Unified Distance Metric for Heterogeneous Attribute Data Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04458)
*Yiqun Zhang,Mingjie Zhao,Yizhou Chen,Yang Lu,Yiu-ming Cheung*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对混合数据聚类，提出异构属性重建与表示(HARR)学习范式，将异构属性转化为同构状态进行距离度量学习，并与聚类集成以自适应不同任务。该方法通过投影到多个可学习空间精细表示分类数据，在准确性和效率方面表现优越。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实聚类任务中常包含数值型和分类型属性（混合数据），这两类属性具有本质差异：数值属性在欧氏距离空间中有明确定义，而分类属性值则是嵌入隐式空间的不同概念。现有方法要么将异构属性编码为单一类型，要么为混合数据定义统一度量，均未揭示其内在联系。同时利用这两种截然不同的信息是一个不可避免但充满挑战的问题。

Method: 提出异构属性重建与表示(HARR)学习范式：1)将异构属性转化为同构状态以进行距离度量学习；2)将度量学习与聚类集成，自动适应不同聚类任务；3)不同于直接采用定义的距离度量或学习属性权重，将每个属性的值投影到统一的可学习多重空间，更精细地表示和学习分类数据的距离度量。该方法无参数、收敛有保证，并能更有效地自适应不同的目标聚类数k。

Result: 大量实验表明，HARR方法在准确性和效率方面均具有优越性。该方法能够更有效地自适应不同的目标聚类数k，且具有参数无关和收敛保证的特性。

Conclusion: HARR范式成功揭示了任意类型属性之间的联系，通过将异构属性转化为同构状态并集成度量学习与聚类，有效解决了混合数据聚类中的核心挑战，为混合数据聚类提供了一种新的解决方案。

Abstract: Datasets composed of numerical and categorical attributes (also called mixed data hereinafter) are common in real clustering tasks. Differing from numerical attributes that indicate tendencies between two concepts (e.g., high and low temperature) with their values in well-defined Euclidean distance space, categorical attribute values are different concepts (e.g., different occupations) embedded in an implicit space. Simultaneously exploiting these two very different types of information is an unavoidable but challenging problem, and most advanced attempts either encode the heterogeneous numerical and categorical attributes into one type, or define a unified metric for them for mixed data clustering, leaving their inherent connection unrevealed. This paper, therefore, studies the connection among any-type of attributes and proposes a novel Heterogeneous Attribute Reconstruction and Representation (HARR) learning paradigm accordingly for cluster analysis. The paradigm transforms heterogeneous attributes into a homogeneous status for distance metric learning, and integrates the learning with clustering to automatically adapt the metric to different clustering tasks. Differing from most existing works that directly adopt defined distance metrics or learn attribute weights to search clusters in a subspace. We propose to project the values of each attribute into unified learnable multiple spaces to more finely represent and learn the distance metric for categorical data. HARR is parameter-free, convergence-guaranteed, and can more effectively self-adapt to different sought number of clusters $k$. Extensive experiments illustrate its superiority in terms of accuracy and efficiency.

Abstract: The quadratic complexity of self-attention during the prefill phase impedes long-context inference in large language models. Existing sparse attention methods face a trade-off among context adaptivity, sampling overhead, and fine-tuning costs. We propose VSPrefill, a mechanism requiring lightweight training that uses the vertical-slash structural pattern in attention distributions. Our compact VSIndexer module predicts context-aware importance scores for vertical columns and slash diagonals from key-value representations augmented with RoPE. This approach constructs sparse masks with linear complexity without modifying the backbone parameters. Evaluated on Qwen3-4B-Instruct and LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct across the LongBench and RULER benchmarks, VSPrefill preserves 98.35% of the full attention accuracy while delivering a 4.95x average speedup at a context length of 128k. ### [179] [Understanding the Dynamics of Demonstration Conflict in In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04464)
*Difan Jiao,Di Wang,Lijie Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型在上下文学习中面对冲突示例时的脆弱性，发现单个错误示例即可导致性能显著下降，并通过机制分析识别出了导致推理失败的两个阶段及关键注意力头。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 上下文学习使大型语言模型能够通过少样本演示执行新任务，但演示本身可能包含噪声和冲突示例。作者旨在理解模型如何处理这些冲突，以及为什么模型在面对相互矛盾的证据时会表现出系统性误导行为。

Method: 作者研究了依赖演示的规则推断任务，使用线性探针和logit lens分析模型内部处理冲突证据的机制，并识别出两个阶段的注意力头：早期至中层的"脆弱头"和晚层的"易感头"。通过针对性消融实验验证发现。

Result: 发现单个损坏规则的演示会导致模型性能大幅下降。模型在损坏情况下会在中间层编码正确和错误两种规则，但仅在晚期层形成预测置信度，呈现出两阶段计算结构。识别出脆弱头对位置注意力有偏且对损坏高度敏感，易感头在暴露于损坏证据时会显著降低对正确预测的支持。针对性消融少量识别出的注意力头可使性能提升超过10%。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了大型语言模型处理冲突证据时的内部计算结构，识别出导致推理失败的关键注意力头，并通过实验验证了干预这些注意力头可以有效缓解模型的脆弱性，为理解和改进模型的上下文学习鲁棒性提供了重要见解。

Abstract: In-context learning enables large language models to perform novel tasks through few-shot demonstrations. However, demonstrations per se can naturally contain noise and conflicting examples, making this capability vulnerable. To understand how models process such conflicts, we study demonstration-dependent tasks requiring models to infer underlying patterns, a process we characterize as rule inference. We find that models suffer substantial performance degradation from a single demonstration with corrupted rule. This systematic misleading behavior motivates our investigation of how models process conflicting evidence internally. Using linear probes and logit lens analysis, we discover that under corruption models encode both correct and incorrect rules in intermediate layers but develop prediction confidence only in late layers, revealing a two-phase computational structure. We then identify attention heads for each phase underlying the reasoning failures: Vulnerability Heads in early-to-middle layers exhibit positional attention bias with high sensitivity to corruption, while Susceptible Heads in late layers significantly reduce support for correct predictions when exposed to the corrupted evidence. Targeted ablation validates our findings, with masking a small number of identified heads improving performance by over 10%.

### [180] [Towards Explainable Deep Learning for Ship Trajectory Prediction in Inland Waterways](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04472)
*Tom Legel,Dirk Söffker,Roland Schätzle,Kathrin Donandt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于LSTM的内河航道船舶轨迹预测模型，通过融合训练的船舶领域参数来增强模型的可解释性。虽然模型在5分钟预测范围内达到了约40米的位移误差，表现与同类研究相当，但研究发现船舶间注意力机制带来的精度提升并非完全源于相邻船舶轨迹之间的因果关系，这一发现突显了内在可解释性设计在揭示模型逻辑方面的重要价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在拥挤的内河航道环境中，准确的船舶轨迹预测对交通安全至关重要。尽管深度学习在复杂场景预测方面展现出优势，但这些模型的可解释性常被忽视，可能掩盖错误的推理逻辑并削弱对模型可靠性的信心。现有研究主要关注船舶间感知能力的提升，而缺乏对模型决策机制的深入理解。

Method: 采用基于LSTM的船舶轨迹预测架构，融合注意力机制来处理交互船舶的隐藏状态。引入训练的船舶领域参数，通过分析注意力权重分布来揭示模型如何关注周围船舶。使用标准位移误差统计量评估预测性能，并分析生成的船舶领域值的合理性。基于内河航道中多样化且复杂的相遇场景进行深入的可解释性分析。

Result: 模型在5分钟预测范围内的最终位移误差约为40米，与同类研究表现相当。船舶间注意力架构确实提升了预测精度，但学习到的船舶领域值所确定的注意力权重与预期存在偏差。这表明观察到的精度改进并非完全由预测轨迹与附近船舶轨迹之间的因果关系驱动。模型成功揭示了注意力机制的实际工作方式，证明了内在可解释性设计的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究强调了可解释性在船舶轨迹预测模型中的重要性。通过内在可解释性设计，研究发现注意力机制的性能提升来源与预期不同，这为理解模型行为提供了关键洞察。未来工作将聚焦于利用该架构进行反事实分析，并纳入更复杂的注意力机制以进一步提升模型的可解释性和预测能力。

Abstract: Accurate predictions of ship trajectories in crowded environments are essential to ensure safety in inland waterways traffic. Recent advances in deep learning promise increased accuracy even for complex scenarios. While the challenge of ship-to-ship awareness is being addressed with growing success, the explainability of these models is often overlooked, potentially obscuring an inaccurate logic and undermining the confidence in their reliability. This study examines an LSTM-based vessel trajectory prediction model by incorporating trained ship domain parameters that provide insight into the attention-based fusion of the interacting vessels' hidden states. This approach has previously been explored in the field of maritime shipping, yet the variety and complexity of encounters in inland waterways allow for a more profound analysis of the model's interpretability. The prediction performance of the proposed model variants are evaluated using standard displacement error statistics. Additionally, the plausibility of the generated ship domain values is analyzed. With an final displacement error of around 40 meters in a 5-minute prediction horizon, the model performs comparably to similar studies. Though the ship-to-ship attention architecture enhances prediction accuracy, the weights assigned to vessels in encounters using the learnt ship domain values deviate from the expectation. The observed accuracy improvements are thus not entirely driven by a causal relationship between a predicted trajectory and the trajectories of nearby ships. This finding underscores the model's explanatory capabilities through its intrinsically interpretable design. Future work will focus on utilizing the architecture for counterfactual analysis and on the incorporation of more sophisticated attention mechanisms.

</details>


### [181] [Activity Recognition from Smart Insole Sensor Data Using a Circular Dilated CNN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04477)
*Yanhua Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于圆形扩张卷积神经网络(CDCNN)的活动分类系统，用于处理智能鞋垫中的多模态时间序列数据，在四类活动分类任务中达到86.42%的测试准确率，适用于嵌入式部署和实时推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能鞋垫配备了压力传感器、加速度计和陀螺仪，为监测人体步态和姿势提供了一种非侵入式手段。为了有效利用这些多模态时间序列数据进行人体活动识别，需要开发一种能够处理此类数据且适合嵌入式部署的分类系统。

Method: 提出了一种基于圆形扩张卷积神经网络(CDCNN)的活动分类系统。该模型处理来自智能鞋垫的多模态时间序列数据，输入为160帧窗口和24个通道（18个压力传感器、3个加速度计轴、3个陀螺仪轴）。采用受试者无关的评估方式，并与基于扁平化数据训练的极端梯度提升树(XGBoost)模型进行对比。同时使用置换特征重要性方法分析不同传感器的贡献。

Result: 在四类活动分类任务（站立、行走、坐着、串联行走）中，CDCNN模型在受试者无关评估中达到86.42%的测试准确率，而XGBoost模型的准确率为87.83%。通过置换特征重要性分析发现，惯性传感器（加速度计和陀螺仪）对分类判别具有显著贡献。

Conclusion: 所提出的CDCNN方法适用于嵌入式部署和实时推理，虽然在准确率上略低于XGBoost模型，但能够有效处理多模态时间序列数据，为智能鞋垫的活动识别提供了一种可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Smart insoles equipped with pressure sensors, accelerometers, and gyroscopes offer a non-intrusive means of monitoring human gait and posture. We present an activity classification system based on a circular dilated convolutional neural network (CDCNN) that processes multi-modal time-series data from such insoles. The model operates on 160-frame windows with 24 channels (18 pressure, 3 accelerometer, 3 gyroscope axes), achieving 86.42% test accuracy in a subject-independent evaluation on a four-class task (Standing, Walking, Sitting, Tandem), compared with 87.83% for an extreme gradient-boosted tree (XGBoost) model trained on flattened data. Permutation feature importance reveals that inertial sensors (accelerometer and gyroscope) contribute substantially to discrimination. The approach is suitable for embedded deployment and real-time inference.

### [183] [Standing on the Shoulders of Giants: Rethinking EEG Foundation Model Pretraining via Multi-Teacher Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04478)
*Chenqi Li,Yu Liu,Shuo Zhang,Timothy Denison,Tingting Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出多教师蒸馏预训练框架（MTDP），利用视觉和时间序列基础模型指导EEG基础模型预训练，在仅用25%预训练数据的情况下优于自监督方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EEG基础模型主要依赖自监督掩码重建，但EEG数据采集成本高、信噪比低，导致模型难以扩展并难以通过重建捕捉潜在神经语义。而图像和文本等模态的基础模型已成熟且表现优异。

Method: 提出两阶段多教师蒸馏预训练框架：第一阶段通过可学习门控网络融合来自不同教师（如DINOv3和Chronos）的表征，采用掩码潜在去噪目标；第二阶段将融合后的表征蒸馏到EEG基础模型中。

Result: 在9个下游任务和12个数据集上的广泛评估表明，基于MTDP的EEG基础模型仅需25%的预训练数据即可超越自监督基线方法，且主流基础模型（视觉和时间序列）能够有效迁移至EEG领域。

Conclusion: 利用成熟模态的基础模型通过多教师蒸馏可以有效引导EEG基础模型预训练，显著降低数据需求并提升性能，为EEG基础模型预训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: Pretraining for electroencephalogram (EEG) foundation models has predominantly relied on self-supervised masked reconstruction, a paradigm largely adapted from and inspired by the success of vision and language foundation models. However, unlike images and text, EEG datasets are notoriously expensive to collect and characterized by low signal-to-noise ratio. These challenges introduce difficulties in scaling the EEG foundation models and capturing the underlying neural semantics through reconstruction. In this work, we ask the question: can we stand on the shoulders of well-established foundation models from well-represented modalities to bootstrap the pretraining of EEG foundation models? We first demonstrate that mainstream foundation models, such as those from vision and time series, transfer surprisingly well to EEG domain. To this end, we propose the Multi-Teacher Distillation Pretraining (MTDP) framework for pretraining EEG foundation models via a two-stage multi-teacher distillation. In the first stage, we introduce a learnable gating network to fuse representations from diverse teachers (e.g., DINOv3 and Chronos) via a masked latent denoising objective. In the second stage, we distill the fused representation into an EEG foundation model. Extensive evaluations across 9 downstream tasks and 12 datasets demonstrate that our MTDP-based EEG foundation model outperforms its self-supervised counterparts while requiring only 25% of the pretraining data.

### [184] [Augmenting representations with scientific papers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04516)
*Nicolò Oreste Pinciroli Vago,Rocco Di Tella,Carolina Cuesta-Lázaro,Michael J. Smith,Cecilia Garraffo,Rafael Martínez-Galarza*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个对比学习框架，用于对齐X射线光谱与科学文献中的领域知识，实现了跨模态检索和多模态融合表征，提升了物理变量估计性能并识别出重要观测目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天文学积累了大量多模态数据（图像、光谱、时间序列）和丰富的文献资料，但这些数据源很少被系统地整合。科学文本包含比光谱更广泛的物理背景信息，建立光谱与文本之间的连接具有内在复杂性。

Method: 提出一个对比学习管道（contrastive pipeline），用于对齐X射线光谱与科学文献文本，构建共享的多模态潜在空间。采用混合专家（Mixture of Experts, MoE）策略，同时利用单模态和共享表征。

Result: 在从光谱检索文本的任务中达到20%的Recall@1%；通过融合光谱和文本数据，对20个物理变量的估计相比单模态光谱基线提升16-18%；共享潜在空间有效编码了物理显著信息；异常分析识别出一个候选脉冲超亮X射线源（PULX）和一个引力透镜系统。

Conclusion: 该方法证明了光谱与文本模态之间有意义对齐的可行性，能够加速对罕见或未被充分理解天体的解释。该框架可扩展到其他能够将观测数据与现有文献对齐的科学领域。

Abstract: Astronomers have acquired vast repositories of multimodal data, including images, spectra, and time series, complemented by decades of literature that analyzes astrophysical sources. Still, these data sources are rarely systematically integrated. This work introduces a contrastive learning framework designed to align X-ray spectra with domain knowledge extracted from scientific literature, facilitating the development of shared multimodal representations. Establishing this connection is inherently complex, as scientific texts encompass a broader and more diverse physical context than spectra. We propose a contrastive pipeline that achieves a 20% Recall@1% when retrieving texts from spectra, proving that a meaningful alignment between these modalities is not only possible but capable of accelerating the interpretation of rare or poorly understood sources. Furthermore, the resulting shared latent space effectively encodes physically significant information. By fusing spectral and textual data, we improve the estimation of 20 physical variables by 16-18% over unimodal spectral baselines. Our results indicate that a Mixture of Experts (MoE) strategy, which leverages both unimodal and shared representations, yields superior performance. Finally, outlier analysis within the multimodal latent space identifies high-priority targets for follow-up investigation, including a candidate pulsating ULX (PULX) and a gravitational lens system. Importantly, this framework can be extended to other scientific domains where aligning observational data with existing literature is possible.

### [185] [Invariant Causal Routing for Governing Social Norms in Online Market Economies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04534)
*Xiangning Yu,Qirui Mi,Xiao Xue,Haoxuan Li,Yiwei Shi,Xiaowei Liu,Mengyue Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了不变因果路由（ICR）框架，用于识别和治理在线市场中的社会规范，通过因果不变性实现跨环境的稳定政策制定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线市场经济中的社会规范（如公平曝光、持续参与、平衡再投资）对长期稳定性至关重要，但这些规范源于无数微观交互的宏观涌现，导致因果归因困难且政策难以跨环境迁移。现有方法难以区分真实因果效应与伪相关。

Method: 提出不变因果路由（ICR）因果治理框架，该框架整合反事实推理与不变因果发现，从异构环境中识别稳定的政策-规范关系，分离真实因果效应与伪相关，构建可解释、可审计且在分布偏移下保持有效的政策规则。

Result: 在基于真实数据校准的异构智能体仿真中，ICR相比相关性或覆盖基线方法，能够产生更稳定的规范、更小的泛化差距以及更简洁的规则。

Conclusion: 因果不变性为治理提供了原则性且可解释的基础，ICR框架能够有效识别跨环境稳定的因果关系，为在线市场的规范治理提供了可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Social norms are stable behavioral patterns that emerge endogenously within economic systems through repeated interactions among agents. In online market economies, such norms -- like fair exposure, sustained participation, and balanced reinvestment -- are critical for long-term stability. We aim to understand the causal mechanisms driving these emergent norms and to design principled interventions that can steer them toward desired outcomes. This is challenging because norms arise from countless micro-level interactions that aggregate into macro-level regularities, making causal attribution and policy transferability difficult. To address this, we propose \textbf{Invariant Causal Routing (ICR)}, a causal governance framework that identifies policy-norm relations stable across heterogeneous environments. ICR integrates counterfactual reasoning with invariant causal discovery to separate genuine causal effects from spurious correlations and to construct interpretable, auditable policy rules that remain effective under distribution shift. In heterogeneous agent simulations calibrated with real data, ICR yields more stable norms, smaller generalization gaps, and more concise rules than correlation or coverage baselines, demonstrating that causal invariance offers a principled and interpretable foundation for governance.

### [186] [An LLM-Guided Query-Aware Inference System for GNN Models on Large Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04545)
*Waleed Afandi,Hussein Abdallah,Ashraf Aboulnaga,Essam Mansour*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KG-WISE提出了一种面向任务的知识图谱推理范式，通过将GNN模型分解为细粒度组件并利用LLM生成查询模板，实现基于查询结构的部分模型加载，在六个大规模知识图谱上实现最高28倍推理加速和98%内存降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GNN推理加速方法（如剪枝、量化、知识蒸馏）无法根据单个查询的结构或语义进行自适应调整；模型以整体文件形式存储，必须完全加载，导致在大规模知识图谱上存在过度的数据加载和冗余计算问题。

Method: 提出KG-WISE方法：1）将训练好的GNN模型分解为细粒度组件，支持根据查询子图结构进行部分加载；2）利用大语言模型（LLM）生成可复用的查询模板，为每个任务提取语义相关的子图；3）实现查询感知的紧凑模型实例化。

Result: 在最多包含4200万节点和1.66亿条边的六个大规模知识图谱上进行评估，KG-WISE相比最先进的系统实现最高28倍推理加速、98%内存使用降低，同时在商业和开源权重LLM上保持或提升准确率。

Conclusion: KG-WISE通过任务驱动的推理范式，有效解决了大规模知识图谱上GNN推理效率问题，证明了细粒度模型分解与LLM驱动的查询模板生成相结合能够显著提升推理性能并降低资源消耗。

Abstract: Efficient inference for graph neural networks (GNNs) on large knowledge graphs (KGs) is essential for many real-world applications. GNN inference queries are computationally expensive and vary in complexity, as each involves a different number of target nodes linked to subgraphs of diverse densities and structures. Existing acceleration methods, such as pruning, quantization, and knowledge distillation, instantiate smaller models but do not adapt them to the structure or semantics of individual queries. They also store models as monolithic files that must be fully loaded, and miss the opportunity to retrieve only the neighboring nodes and corresponding model components that are semantically relevant to the target nodes. These limitations lead to excessive data loading and redundant computation on large KGs. This paper presents KG-WISE, a task-driven inference paradigm for large KGs. KG-WISE decomposes trained GNN models into fine-grained components that can be partially loaded based on the structure of the queried subgraph. It employs large language models (LLMs) to generate reusable query templates that extract semantically relevant subgraphs for each task, enabling query-aware and compact model instantiation. We evaluate KG-WISE on six large KGs with up to 42 million nodes and 166 million edges. KG-WISE achieves up to 28x faster inference and 98% lower memory usage than state-of-the-art systems while maintaining or improving accuracy across both commercial and open-weight LLMs.

</details>


### [187] [Oracle-efficient Hybrid Learning with Constrained Adversaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04546)
*Princewill Okoroafor,Robert Kleinberg,Michael P. Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了混合在线学习问题，提出了一种新的高效算法，在给定ERM预言机的情况下，首次同时实现了统计最优性和计算效率，并将结果应用于随机零和博弈的均衡计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合在线学习问题（特征服从未知分布，标签由对手生成）介于统计学习和完全对抗性在线学习之间。先前研究存在两难困境：统计最优的算法计算上不可行，而计算高效的算法统计上次优。本文旨在打破这一困境，同时实现统计最优性和计算效率。

Method: 考虑结构化设置，限制对手从固定的函数类R中选择标签。提出新算法，使用ERM预言机高效运行。开发了多项技术工具：带有"截断熵正则化器"的新型Frank-Wolfe归约，以及针对"混合"鞅差序列之和的新尾界。

Result: 算法的遗憾界与由学习者的假设类H和对手的标签类R导出的类的Rademacher复杂度相关。作为关键推论，给出了在随机零和博弈中计算均衡的预言机高效算法，适用于动作集高维但支付函数具有低维结构的情况。

Conclusion: 本文在混合学习设置中取得了重要进展，首次实现了统计最优性和计算效率的统一，为结构化对抗环境下的在线学习提供了新的理论工具和算法框架。

Abstract: The Hybrid Online Learning Problem, where features are drawn i.i.d. from an unknown distribution but labels are generated adversarially, is a well-motivated setting positioned between statistical and fully-adversarial online learning. Prior work has presented a dichotomy: algorithms that are statistically-optimal, but computationally intractable (Wu et al., 2023), and algorithms that are computationally-efficient (given an ERM oracle), but statistically-suboptimal (Wu et al., 2024).
  This paper takes a significant step towards achieving statistical optimality and computational efficiency simultaneously in the Hybrid Learning setting. To do so, we consider a structured setting, where the Adversary is constrained to pick labels from an expressive, but fixed, class of functions $R$. Our main result is a new learning algorithm, which runs efficiently given an ERM oracle and obtains regret scaling with the Rademacher complexity of a class derived from the Learner's hypothesis class $H$ and the Adversary's label class $R$. As a key corollary, we give an oracle-efficient algorithm for computing equilibria in stochastic zero-sum games when action sets may be high-dimensional but the payoff function exhibits a type of low-dimensional structure. Technically, we develop a number of tools for the design and analysis of our learning algorithm, including a novel Frank-Wolfe reduction with "truncated entropy regularizer" and a new tail bound for sums of "hybrid" martingale difference sequences.

</details>


### [188] [Latent Particle World Models: Self-supervised Object-centric Stochastic Dynamics Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04553)
*Tal Daniel,Carl Qi,Dan Haramati,Amir Zadeh,Chuan Li,Aviv Tamar,Deepak Pathak,David Held*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了LPWM，一种可扩展到真实世界多物体数据集的自监督物体中心世界模型，能够从视频中无监督地发现关键点、边界框和物体掩码，并支持动作、语言和图像目标的灵活条件控制，在随机视频建模和目标条件模仿学习等决策任务中达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的物体中心世界模型难以扩展到真实世界的多物体数据集，且在决策任务中的应用受限。本文旨在开发一种能够自主发现物体表示、支持多种条件输入、并适用于真实场景的自监督世界模型。

Method: 提出Latent Particle World Model (LPWM)架构，通过自监督方式从视频中自动发现关键点、边界框和物体掩码；设计新颖的潜在动作模块来建模随机粒子动力学；整个系统端到端训练，支持动作、语言和图像目标的灵活条件控制。

Result: 在多样化的真实世界和合成数据集上达到最先进(SOTA)性能；成功应用于随机视频建模任务；在目标条件模仿学习等决策任务中验证了模型的有效性。

Conclusion: LPWM成功地将物体中心世界模型扩展到真实世界场景，证明了自监督学习的物体表示在视频建模和决策任务中的强大能力，为未来研究提供了代码、数据、预训练模型和视频演示。

Abstract: We introduce Latent Particle World Model (LPWM), a self-supervised object-centric world model scaled to real-world multi-object datasets and applicable in decision-making. LPWM autonomously discovers keypoints, bounding boxes, and object masks directly from video data, enabling it to learn rich scene decompositions without supervision. Our architecture is trained end-to-end purely from videos and supports flexible conditioning on actions, language, and image goals. LPWM models stochastic particle dynamics via a novel latent action module and achieves state-of-the-art results on diverse real-world and synthetic datasets. Beyond stochastic video modeling, LPWM is readily applicable to decision-making, including goal-conditioned imitation learning, as we demonstrate in the paper. Code, data, pre-trained models and video rollouts are available: https://taldatech.github.io/lpwm-web
